vṛṣyāya vṛṣṇaye vṛṣaṇāya ca kaṭaṅkaṭāya caṇḍāya namaḥ sa avayavāya ca namaḥ te vara kṛṣṇāya varāya vara dāya ca namaḥ varṣāya vātāya chāyāyai ātapāya ca namaḥ rakta viraktāya śobhanāya akṣa māline namaḥ śivāya śāntāya namaḥ śāntatarāya ca namaḥ vṛddhāya lubdhāya saṃvibhāga priyāya ca pañcamālā arcita aṅgāya namaḥ pāśupatāya ca namaḥ caṇḍāya ghaṇṭāya ghaṇṭayā jagdha randhriṇe sahasa śataghaṇṭāya ghaṇṭā mālā priyāya ca prāṇa daṇḍāya tyāgāya namaḥ hilihilāya ca hūṃhūṅkārāya pārāya hūṃhūṅkāra priyāya ca namaḥ ca śambhave nityam giri vṛkṣa kalāya ca garbha māṃsa śrṛgālāya tārakāya tarāya ca yajña vāhāya dānāya tapyāya tapanāya ca namaḥ taṭāya bhavyāya taḍitām pataye namaḥ namaḥ sahasra śīrṣṇe ca sahasra caraṇāya ca namaḥ astu bāla rūpāya bāla rūpa dharāya ca bālānām ca eva goptre ca bāla krīḍanakāya ca namaḥ śuddhāya buddhāya kṣobhaṇāya akṣatāya ca taraṅga aṅkita keśāya muktakeśāya vai namaḥ namaḥ ṣaṭkarma niṣṭāya trikarma niratāya ca varṇa āśramāṇām vidhivat pṛthak karma pravartine manaḥ ghoṣāya ghoṣyāya namaḥ kalakalāya ca śveta piṅgala netrāya kṛṣṇa rakta kṣaṇāya ca dharma artha kāma mokṣāya krathāya kathanāya ca sāṅkhyāya sāṅkhya mukhyāya yoga adhipataye namaḥ kṛṣṇā jina uttarīyāya vyāla yajña upavītine īśāna vajra saṃhāya harikeśa namaḥ astu te kāma kāma da kāmadhna dhṛṣṭa udṛpta niṣūdana mahā bāla mahā bāho mahā sattva mahā dyute valkala ajina dhāriṇe dīpta śūrya agni jaṭine valkala ajina vāsase unmādana śata āvartta gaṅgā toya arddha mūrddhajaḥ sattvasya paramā yoniḥ ap vāyu jyotiṣām nidhiḥ ṛk sāmani tathā uṅkāram āhuḥ tvām brahma vādinaḥ haviḥ hāvī havaḥ hāvī huvām vācā āhutiḥ sadā gāyanti tvām sura śreṣṭha sāma gāḥ brahma vādinaḥ paṭyase brahma vidbhiḥ tvam kalpa upaniṣadām gaṇaiḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ varṇa avarāḥ ca ye saṃvatsaraḥ tvam ṛtavaḥ māsāḥ māsa arddham eva ca kalā kāṣṭā nimeṣāḥ ca nakṣatrāṇi yugāḥ grahāḥ vṛṣāṇām kakudam tvam higirīṇām śikharāṇi ca siṃhaḥ mṛgāṇām patatām tārkṣyaḥ anantaḥ ca bhoginām kṣīrodaḥ hi udadhīnām ca yantrāṇām dhanuḥ eva ca vajram praharaṇānām ca vratānām satyam eva ca icchā dveṣaḥ ca rāgaḥ ca mohaḥ kṣāmaḥ damaḥ śamaḥ tvam gadī tvam śarī ca api khaṭvāṅgī jharjharī tathā daśa lakṣaṇa saṃyuktaḥ dharmaḥ arthaḥ kāmaḥ eva indraḥ samudrāḥ saritaḥ palvalāni sarāṃsi ca latā vallī tṛṇa oṣadhyaḥ paśavaḥ mṛga pakṣiṇaḥ ādiśva antaḥ ca madhyaḥ ca gāyatrī oṅkāraḥ eva ca haritaḥ lohitaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ nīlaḥ pītaḥ tathā aruṇaḥ suvarṇaretāḥ vikhyātaḥ suvarṇaḥ ca api atas mataḥ suparṇam ca tathā brahma yajuṣām śatarudriyam pavitrāṇām pavitram ca maṅgalānām ca maṅgalam giriḥ stokaḥ tathā vṛkṣaḥ jīvaḥ pudgalaḥ eva ca prāṇaḥ apānaḥ sāmānaḥ ca udānaḥ vyānaḥ eva ca unmeṣaḥ ca eva meṣaḥ ca tathā jṛmbhitam eva ca lohita aṅgaḥ gadī daṃṣṭrī mahā vaktraḥ mahā udaraḥ matsyaḥ jalī jalaḥ jalya javaḥ kālaḥ kalī kalaḥ vikālaḥ ca sukālaḥ ca duṣkālaḥ kalanāśanaḥ mṛtyuḥ ca eva kṣayaḥ antaḥ ca kṣamā apāya karaḥ haraḥ ghaṭaḥ ghaṭīkaḥ ghaṇṭīko cūḍā lola balaḥ balam brahmakālaḥ agnivaktraḥ ca daṇḍī muṇḍī ca daṇḍadhṛk caturā śrama vettā ca cāturvarṇya karaḥ ca ha śilpīśaḥ śilpinām śreṣṭhaḥ sarva śilpa pravarttakaḥ bhaga netra antakaḥ candraḥ pūṣṇaḥ danta vināśanaḥ gūḍha āvarttaḥ ca gūḍhaḥ ca gūḍha pratiniṣevitā taraṇaḥ tā rakaḥ ca eva sarva bhūta su tāraṇaḥ dhātā vidhātā satvānām nidhātā dhāraṇaḥ dharaḥ īśānaḥ vīkṣaṇaḥ śāntaḥ durdāntaḥ dantanāśanaḥ kāma bimba niharttā ca karṇikāra rajaḥ priyaḥ hiraṇyagarbhaḥ śakuniḥ mahā udadhiḥ paraḥ virāj gotamaḥ gopratāraḥ ca govṛṣeḥ caravāhanaḥ tiṣṭhan sthiraḥ ca sthāṇuḥ ca niṣkampaḥ kampaḥ eva ca śaśaḥ śaśāṅkaḥ śamanaḥ śīta uṣṇam durjarā atha tṛṣ ādhayaḥ vyādhayaḥ ca eva vyādhi hā vyādhi gaḥ ca ha sahyaḥ yajñaḥ mṛgāḥ vyādhāḥ vyādhīnām ākaraḥ akaraḥ śikhaṇḍī puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ puṇḍarīkāvalokanaḥ daṇḍa dharaḥ sa daṇḍaḥ ca daṇḍa muṇḍa vibhūṣitaḥ viṣapaḥ amṛtapaḥ ca eva surāpaḥ kṣīrasomapaḥ madhupaḥ ca ājyapaḥ ca eva sarvapaḥ ca mahā balaḥ vṛṣa aśva vāhyaḥ vṛṣabhaḥ tathā vṛṣabha locanaḥ vṛṣabhaḥ ca eva vikhyātaḥ lokānām loka satkṛtaḥ candra ādityau cakṣuṣī te hṛdayañca pitāmahaḥ na brahmā na ca govindaḥ purāṇ ṛṣayaḥ na ca māhātmyam veditum śaktāḥ yāthātathyena te yāḥ mūrttayaḥ su sūkṣmāḥ te na mahyam yānti darśanam tābhiḥ nām satatam rakṣa pitā putram iva aurasam rakṣa mām rakṣaṇīyaḥ aham tava anagha namaḥ astu te bhakta anukampī bhagavān bhaktaḥ ca aham sadā tvayi yaḥ sahasrāṇi anekāni puṃsām āhṛtya durddaśaḥ tiṣṭhati ekaḥ samudra ante sa me goptā astu nityaśas yam vinidrāḥ jita śvāsāḥ sattva sthāḥ sama darśinaḥ jyotiḥ paśyanti yuñjānāḥ tasmai yoga ātmane namaḥ ye aṅguṣṭha mātrāḥ puruṣāḥ deha sthāḥ sarva dehinām rakṣantu te hi mām nityam nityam āpyāyayantu mām ye ca api utpatitāḥ garbhāt adhobhāga gatāḥ ca ye teṣām svāhāḥ svadhāḥ ca eva āpnuvantu svadantu ca vṛkṣa mūleṣu goṣṭeṣu kāntāra gahaneṣu rasātala gatāḥ ye ca ye ca tasmāt paraṅga tāḥ sūkṣmāḥ sthūlāḥ kṛśāḥ hrasvāḥ namaḥ tebhyaḥ tu nityaśas atha vā māyayā deva mohitaḥ sūkṣmayā tvayā etasmāt kāraṇāt vā api tena tvam na nimantritaḥ tvam gatiḥ tvam pratiṣṭā ca na ca anyā asti na me gatiḥ stutvā evam sa mahādevam virarāma prajāpātiḥ bhagavān api su prītaḥ punar dakṣam abhāṣata kṛtvā āśvāsa karam vākyam vākya jñaḥ vākyam āhatam aham yajña hā na tu anyaḥ dṛśyate tat purā tvayā bhūyas ca tam varam imam mattaḥ gṛhṇīṣva suvrata prasanna vadanaḥ bhūtvā tvam ekāgra manāḥ śrṛṇu prajāpate mad prasādāt phala bhāgī bhaviṣyasi vedān ṣaṣ aṅgān uddhṛtya sāṅkhyān yogān ca kṛtsnaśas tapaḥ ca vipulam taptvā duścaram deva dānavaiḥ varṇa āśrama kṛtaiḥ dharmaiḥ viparītam kvacid samam śruti arthaiḥ adhyavasitam paśu pāśa vimokṣaṇam sarveṣām āśramāṇām tu mayā pāśupatam vratam utpāditam śubham dakṣa sarva pāpa vimokṣaṇam tat astu te mahābhāga mānasaḥ tyajyatām jvaraḥ evam uktvā mahādevaḥ sa patnīkaḥ saha anugaḥ avāpya ca tadā bhāgam yathoktam brahmaṇā bhavaḥ śānti artham sarva bhūtānām śrṛṇudhvam tatra vai dvijāḥ śīrṣa abhitāpaḥ nāgānām parvatānām śilā rujaḥ nālikām vidyāt nirmokam bhujageṣu api śaurakaḥ saurabheyāṇām ūṣaraḥ pṛthivī tale ibhāḥ nām api dharma jña dṛṣṭi pratyavarodhanam randhra udbhūtam tathā aśvānām śikhā udbhedaḥ ca barhiṇām netra rogaḥ kokilānām jvaraḥ proktaḥ mahātmabhiḥ ajānām pitta bhedaḥ ca sarveṣām iti naḥ śrutam śukānām api sarveṣām himikā procyate jvaraḥ śārdūleṣu api vai viprāḥ śramaḥ jvaraḥ iha ucyate mānuṣeṣu tu sarvajña jvaraḥ nāma eṣa kīrtitaḥ etat māheśvaram tejau jvaraḥ nāma su dāruṇaḥ namasyaḥ ca eva mānyaḥ ca sarva prāṇibhiḥ īśvaraḥ imām jvara utpattim adīna mānasaḥ paṭet sadā yaḥ su samāhitaḥ naraḥ dakṣa proktam stavan ca api kīrttayet yaḥ śrṛṇoti na aśubham prāpnuyāt kiñcid dīrgham ca āyuḥ avāpnuyāt yathā sarveṣu deveṣu variṣṭaḥ yogavān haraḥ tathā stavaḥ variṣṭaḥ ayam stavānām brahma nirmitaḥ yaśaḥ rājya sukha aiśvarya vitta āyuḥ dhana kāṅkṣibhiḥ anena ca eva dehena gaṇānām sa gaṇa adhipaḥ na ca yakṣāḥ piśācāḥ vā na nāgāḥ na vināyakāḥ śrṛṇuyāt vai idam nārī subhaktyā brahmacāriṇī pitṛbhiḥ bhartṛ pakṣābhyām pūjyā bhavati deva vat śrṛṇuyāt vai idam sarva kīrttayet vā api abhīkṣṇaśas tasya sarvāṇi kāryāṇi siddhim gacchanti avighnataḥ manasā cintitam yat ca yat ca vācā api udāhṛtam tatas sa yuktaḥ gṛhṇīyāt nāmāni āśu yathākramam īpsitān labhate atyartham kāmān bhogān ca mānavaḥ mṛtaḥ ca svargam āpnoti strī sahasra parivṛtaḥ paṭhan dakṣa kṛtam stotram sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate mṛtaḥ ca gaṇa sālokyam pūjyamānaḥ sura asuraiḥ ā bhūta saṃplava sthāyī rudrasya anucaraḥ bhavet iti āha bhagavān vyāsaḥ parāśara sutaḥ prabhuḥ śrutvā etat paramam guhyam ye api syuḥ pāpa kāriṇaḥ vaiśyāḥ striyaḥ ca śūdrāḥ ca rudra lokam avāpnuyuḥ iti śrī mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte dakṣaśāpavarṇanam nāma triṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca iti eṣā samanujñātā kathā pāpa praṇāśinī yā dakṣam adhikṛtya iha kathā śarvāt upāgatā pitṛ vaṃśa prasaṅgena kathā hi eṣā prakīrtitā pitṝṇām ānupūrvyeṇa devān vakṣyāmi atas param devāḥ yāmāḥ iti khyātāḥ pūrvam ye yajña sūnavaḥ ajitāḥ brahmaṇaḥ putrāḥ jitāḥ jit ajitāḥ ca ye putrāḥ svāyambhuvasya ete śukra nāmnā mānasāḥ tṛptimantaḥ gaṇāḥ hi ete devānām tu trayaḥ smṛtāḥ vāyasaḥ maṅgalaḥ ca eva yāmāḥ dvādaśa kīrtitāḥ abhimanyuḥ ugra dṛṣṭiḥ samayaḥ atha śuciśravāḥ yaminaḥ viśva deva ādyam yaviṣṭaḥ amṛtavān api śrutiśrṛṇaḥ bṛhat śukraḥ devāḥ dvādaśa kīrtitāḥ tviṣimantaḥ gaṇāḥ hi ete vīryavantaḥ mahā balāḥ teṣām indraḥ sadā hi āsīt viśvabhuj prathamaḥ vibhuḥ asurāḥ teṣām āsan dāyāda bāndhavāḥ suparṇa yakṣa gandharvāḥ piśāca uraga rākṣasāḥ aṣṭau te pitṛbhiḥ sārddham nāsatyāḥ deva yonayaḥ svāyambhuve antare atītāḥ prajāḥ tu āsām sahasraśas prabhāva rūpa sampannāḥ āyuṣā ca balena ca svāyambhuvaḥ nisargaḥ ca vijñeyaḥ sāmpratam manuḥ atīte varttamānena dṛṣṭaḥ vaivasvatena saḥ prajābhiḥ devatābhiḥ ca ṛṣibhiḥ pitṛbhiḥ saha teṣām saptarṣayaḥ pūrvam āsan ye tān nibodhata bhṛgu aṅgirāḥ marīciḥ ca pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ agnīdhraḥ ca atibāhuḥ ca medhāḥ medhātithiḥ vasuḥ vāyu proktāḥ mahāsattvāḥ rājānaḥ prathame antare sa piśāca manuṣyam ca suparṇa apsarasā aṅgaṇam no śakyam ānupūrvyeṇa vaktum varṣa śataiḥ api bahu tvāt nāmadheyānām saṅkhyā teṣām kule tathā kālena bahunā atītāḥ ayana abda yuga kramaiḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ kaḥ eṣa bhagavān kālaḥ sarva bhūta apahārakaḥ kim asya cakṣuḥ kā mūrtiḥ ke ca asya avayavāḥ smṛtāḥ kiṃnāmadheyaḥ kaḥ asya ātmā etat prabrūhi pṛcchatām uvāca śrūyatām kāla sadbhāvaḥ śrutvā ca eva avadhāryatām sūrya yoniḥ nimeṣa ādiḥ saṅkhyācakṣuḥ saḥ ucyate mūrttiḥ asya tu ahar rātre nimeṣa avayavaḥ ca saḥ saṃvatsara śatam tu asya nāma ca asya kalā ātmakam sāmprata an āgata atīta kāla ātmā sa prajāpatiḥ pañcānām pravibhaktānām kāla avasthām vatsaraḥ pañcamaḥ teṣām kālaḥ sa yuga saṃjñitaḥ teṣām tu tattvam vakṣyāmi kīrttyamānam nibodhata āditye yaḥ tu asau sāraḥ kālāgniḥ parivatsaraḥ śukla kṛṣṇā gatiḥ ca api apām sāra mayaḥ khagaḥ saḥ iḍā vatsaraḥ somaḥ purāṇe niścayaḥ mataḥ yaḥ ca ayam tapate lokān tanubhiḥ sapta saptabhiḥ ahaṅkārāt rudan rudraḥ sat bhūtaḥ brahmaṇaḥ trayaḥ sa rudraḥ vatsaraḥ teṣām vijajñe nīlalohitaḥ teṣām hi tattvam vakṣyāmi kīrtyamānam nibodhata aṅga pratyaṅga saṃyogāt kāla ātmā prapitāmahaḥ ṛk sāma yajuṣām yoniḥ pañcānām patiḥ īśvaraḥ saḥ agniḥ yajuḥ ca somaḥ ca sa bhūtaḥ sa prajāpatiḥ proktaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ ca iti sūryaḥ yaḥ agniḥ manīṣibhiḥ yasmāt kāla vibhāgānām māsa ṛtu ayanayoḥ api graha nakṣatra śīta uṣṇa varṣa āyuḥ karmaṇām tathā yojitaḥ pravibhāgānām divasānām ca bhāskaraḥ vaikārikaḥ prasanna ātmā brahma putraḥ prajāpatiḥ ādityaḥ savitā bhānuḥ jīvanaḥ brahma satkṛtaḥ prabhavaḥ ca atya yaḥ ca eva bhūtānām tena bhāskaraḥ tārā abhimānī vijñeyaḥ tṛtīyaḥ parivatsaraḥ ājīvaḥ sarva bhūtānām yogakṣema kṛt īśvaraḥ satatam bibharti jagat aṃśubhiḥ tithīnām parvasandhīnām pūrṇimā ādarśayoḥ api yoniḥ niśākaraḥ yaḥ ca yaḥ amṛta ātmā prajāpatiḥ tasmāt sa pitṛmān somaḥ ṛk yajuḥ chanda ātmakaḥ prāṇa apāna samāna ādyaiḥ vyāna udāna ātmakaiḥ api karmabhiḥ prāṇinām loke sarva ceṣṭā pravarttakaḥ prāṇa apāna samānānām vāyūnām ca pravarttakaḥ jala ātmanām samāna kāla karaṇaḥ kriyāḥ sampādayan iva sarva ātmā sarva lokānām āvahaḥ pravaha ādibhiḥ vidhātā sarva bhūtānām kṣamī nityam prabhañjanaḥ yoniḥ agneḥ apām bhūmeḥ raveḥ candramasaḥ cayaḥ vāyuḥ prajāpiḥ bhūtam loka ātmā prapitāmahaḥ gāyatrī ca eva triṣṭubh ca jagatī ca eva yā smṛtā tryambakāḥ nāmataḥ proktāḥ yonayaḥ savanasya tāḥ tābhiḥ eka tva bhūtābhiḥ trividhābhiḥ sva vīryataḥ tri sādhana puroḍāśaḥ tri kapālaḥ sa vai smṛtaḥ iti etat pañca varṣam hi yugam proktam manīṣibhiḥ sā ekam ṣaṭkam vijajñe atha madhu ādīn ṛtavaḥ kila pañca iti sargaḥ samāsatas iti eṣa pavamānaḥ vai prāṇinām jīvitāni tu nadī vega samāyuktam kālaḥ dhāvati saṃharan ete prajānām patayaḥ pradhānāḥ sarva dehinām pitaraḥ sarve lokānām loka ātmānaḥ prakīrtitāḥ ṛṣiḥ vipraḥ mahādevaḥ bhūtātmā prapitāmahaḥ īśvaraḥ sarva bhūtānām praṇavāya upapadyate ātma veśena bhūtānām aṅga pratyaṅga sambhavaḥ agniḥ saṃvatsaraḥ sūryaḥ candramāḥ vāyuḥ eva ca yuga abhimānī kāla ātmā nityam saṃkṣepa kṛt vibhuḥ āśraya āśraya saṃyogāt tanubhiḥ nāmabhiḥ tathā patiḥ patīnām bhagavān prajā īśānām prajāpatiḥ bhavanaḥ sarva bhūtānām sarveṣām nīla lohitaḥ oṣadhīḥ pratisandhatte rudraḥ kṣīṇāḥ punar punar iti eṣām yat apatyam vai na tat śakyam pramāṇataḥ imam vaṃśam prajā īśānām mahatām puṇya karmaṇām kīrttayan sthira kīrttīnām mahatīm siddhim āpnuyāt iti śrī mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte devavaṃśavarṇanam nāma ekatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca oṅkāram akṣaram brahma tri varṇam ca ādeḥ smṛtam ṛcaḥ yajūṃṣi sāmāni vāyuḥ agniḥ tathā jalam caturddaśa mahātmānaḥ devānām ye tu daivatāḥ akṣarāt niḥ sṛtāḥ sarve devadevāt maheśvarāt kṛtam tretā dvāparan ca yugādiḥ kalinā saha devatāḥ tu tadā udvignāḥ kālasya vaśam āgatāḥ na śaknuvanti tat mānam saṃssthāpayitum ātmanā tadā te vāgyatāḥ bhūtvā ādau manvantarasya vai ṛṣayaḥ ca eva devāḥ ca indraḥ ca eva mahā tapāḥ samādhāya manaḥ tīvram sahasram parivatsarān prapannāḥ te mahādevam bhītāḥ kālasya vai tadā ayam hi kālaḥ deveśaḥ catur mūrtiḥ caturmukhaḥ atha dṛṣṭvā mahādevaḥ tam tu kālam caturmukham na bhetavyam iti prāha kaḥ vaḥ kāmaḥ pradīyatām tat kariṣyāmi aham sarvam na vṛthak ayam pariśramaḥ uvāca devaḥ bhagavān svayaṅkālaḥ su durjayaḥ yat etat rakta varṇa ābham tṛtīyam vaḥ smṛtam mayā tri jihvam lelihānam tu etat tretā yugam dvijāḥ iṣṭvā ca eva agnayaḥ viprāḥ kālajihvā pravarttate dvipādaḥ atra bhaviṣyāmi dvāparam nāma tat yugam yat etat kṛṣṇa varṇa ābham turīyam rakta locanam eka jihvam pṛthu śyāmam lelihānam punar punar brahmā kṛta yuge pūjyaḥ tretāyām yajñaḥ icyate dvāpare pūjyate viṣṇuḥ aham pūjyaḥ caturṣu api brahmā viṣṇuḥ ca yajñaḥ ca kālasya eva kalāḥ trayaḥ sarveṣu eva hi kāleṣu catur mūrtiḥ maheśvaraḥ aham janaḥ janayitā kālaḥ kāla pravarttakaḥ yuga kartā tathā ca eva param para parāyaṇaḥ tasmāt kali yugam prāpya lokānām hita kāraṇāt tadā bhavyaḥ ca pūjyaḥ ca bhaviṣyāmi sura uttamāḥ tasmāt bhayam na kāryam ca kalim prāpya mahā ojasaḥ evam uktāḥ statas sarvāḥ devatāḥ ṛṣibhiḥ saha ūcuḥ mahā tejāḥ mahā kāyaḥ mahā vīryaḥ mahā dyutiḥ bhīṣaṇaḥ sarva bhūtānām katham kālaḥ caturmukhaḥ uvāca eṣa kālaḥ catur mūrtiḥ catur daṃṣṭraḥ catur mukhaḥ loka saṃrakṣaṇa arthāya atikrāmati sarvaśas kālaḥ sṛjati bhūtāni punar saṃharati kramāt sarve kālasya vaśa gāḥ na kālaḥ kasyacid vaśe tasmāt tu sarva bhūtāni kālaḥ kalayate sadā tāni manvantarāṇi iha parivṛtta yuga kramāt yadā kālaḥ prakramate tadā manvantara kṣayaḥ evam uktvā tu bhagavān deva ṛṣi pitṛ dānavān evam sa kāle bhagavān deva ṛṣi pitṛ dānavān punar punar saṃharate sṛjate ca punar punar pūjyate bhagavān īśaḥ bhayāt kālasya tasya vai tasmāt devāḥ divam gatvā avatīrya ca bhū tale ṛṣayaḥ ca eva devāḥ ca kalim prāpya su dāruṇam tapaḥ icchanti bhūyiṣṭham karttum dharma parāyaṇāḥ avatārān kalim prāpya karoti ca punar punar evam kāla antare sarve ye atītāḥ vai sahasraśas devāpiḥ poravaḥ rājā manu śva ikṣvāku vaṃśa jāḥ mahā yoga bala upetāḥ kāla antaram upāsate kṣīṇe kali yuge tasmin tiṣye tretā yuge kṛte saptarṣibhiḥ ca eva sārddham bhāvye tretā yuge punar gotrāṇām kṣatriyāṇām ca bhaviṣyāḥ te prakīrtitāḥ dvāpara ante pratiṣṭhante kṣatriyāḥ ṛṣibhiḥ saha kṛte tretā yuge ca eva tathā kṣīṇe ca dvāpare narāḥ pātakinaḥ ye vai varttante te kalau smṛtāḥ manvantarāṇām saptānām sāntāna arthā śrutiḥ smṛtiḥ yathā vai prakṛtiḥ tebhyaḥ pravṛttānām yathā kṣayam jāmadagnyena rāmeṇa kṣatre niravaśoṣite kriyante kulaṭāḥ sarvāḥ kṣatriyaiḥ vasudhādhipaiḥ aiḍam ikṣvāku vaṃśasya prakṛtim paricakṣate rājānaḥ śreṇibandhāḥ tu takṣā anye kṣatriyāḥ bhuvi aiḍa vaṃśe atha sambhūtāḥ yathā ca ikṣvākavaḥ nṛpāḥ tebhyaḥ eva śatam pūrṇam kulānām abhiṣecitam tāvat eva tu bhojānām vistaraḥ dviguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ bhojantu tri śatam kṣatram caturddhā tat yathādiśam teṣu atītāḥ tu rājānaḥ bruvataḥ tān nibodhata śatam vai prativindhyānām haihayānām tathā śatam dhārttarāṣṭrāḥ tu ekaśatam aśītiḥ janamejayāḥ śatam vai brahmadattānām kulānām vīryiṇām śatam tatas śatam tu paulānām śatam kāśi kuśa ādayaḥ tathā aparam ye atītāḥ śaśabindavaḥ ijānāḥ te aśvamedhaiḥ tu sarve niyuta dakṣiṇaiḥ evam saṃkṣepataḥ proktāḥ na śakyāḥ vistareṇa tu vaktum rājarṣayaḥ kṛtsnāḥ ye atītāḥ taiḥ yukaiḥ saha ete yayāti vaṃśasya babhūvuḥ vaṃśa varddhanāḥ āyuḥ putrāḥ dhanam kīrtiḥ aiśvaryam bhūtiḥ eva ca dhāraṇāt śravaṇāt ca eva pañcavargasya dhīmatām catvāri āhuḥ sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām ca kṛtam yugam tasya tāvacchatī sandhyā sandhyā aṃśaḥ ca tathāvidhaḥ kṛte vai prakriyā pādaḥ catuḥsāhasraḥ ucyate tasmāt catuḥśatam sandhyā sandhyā aṃśaḥ ca yathāvidhaḥ tretā ādīni sahasrāṇi saṃkhyayā munibhiḥ saha tasya api triśatī sandhyā sandhyā aṃśaḥ triśataḥ smṛtaḥ anuṣaṅga pādaḥ tretāyāḥ tri sāhasraḥ tu saṅkhyayā dvāpare dve sahasre tu varṣāṇām samprakīrtitam tasya api dviśatī sandhyā sandhyāṃśaḥ dviśataḥ tathā kalim prāhuḥ saṅkhyā vidaḥ janāḥ tasya api śatikā sandhyā sandhyā aṃśaḥ śatam eva ca saṃhāra pādaḥ vai kalau yuge sa sandhyāni saha aṃśāni catvāri tu yugāni vai evam pādaiḥ sahasrāṇi ślokānām pañca pañca ca evam dvādaśa sāhasram purāṇam kavayaḥ viduḥ yathā vedaḥ catuṣpādaḥ catuṣpādam tathā yugam yathā yugam catuṣpādam vidhātrā vihitam svayam cha catuṣpādam surāṇām tu brahmaṇā vihitam purā iti śrī mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte yugadharmanirūpaṇam nāma dvātriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca manvantareṣu sarveṣu atīta anāgateṣu iha tulya abhimāninaḥ sarve jāyante nāma rūpataḥ ṛṣayaḥ mānavāḥ ca eva sarve tulya abhimāninaḥ vistareṇa ānupūrvyā ca kīrttyamānam nibodhata manoḥ svāyambhuvasya āsan daśa pautrāḥ tu tad samāḥ yaiḥ iyam pṛthivī sarvā sapta dvīpa samanvitā priyavratāt prajāvantaḥ vīrāt kanyā vyajāyata kanyā sā tu mahābhāgā karddamasya prajāpateḥ kanye dve śata putrān ca samrāj kukṣiḥ ca te ubhe taryoḥ vai bhrātaraḥ śūrāḥ prajāpati samāḥ daśa agnīdhraḥ ca vapuṣmān ca medhāḥ medhātithiḥ vibhuḥ dvīpeṣu teṣu dharmeṇa dvīpān tān ca nibodhata plakṣadvīpa īśvaraḥ ca api tena medhātithiḥ kṛtaḥ śālmalau tu vapuṣmantam rājānam abhiṣiktavān jyotiṣmantam kuśadvīpe rājānam kṛtavān prabhuḥ dyutimantam ca rājānam kraujcadvīpe samādiśat śākadvīpa īśvaram ca api havyan cakre priyavrataḥ puṣkara adhipatim ca api savanam kṛtavān prabhuḥ mahāvītam smṛtam varṣam tasya nāmnā mahātmanaḥ nāmnā tu dhātakeḥ ca api dhātakīkhaṇḍaḥ ucyate havyaḥ vyajanayat putrān śākadvīpa īśvarān prabhuḥ jaladañca kumārañca su kumāram maṇīcakam kumārasya ca kaumāram dvitīyam parikīrtitam sukumāram sukumārasya kīrtitam modākasya tu modākam varṣam ṣaṣṭham prakīrtitam mānabhiḥ tāni sapta varṣāṇi tatra vai kuśalaḥ manugaḥ ca uṣṇaḥ pīvaraḥ ca andhakārakaḥ teṣām sva nāmabhiḥ ddeśāḥ krauñcadvīpa āśrayāḥ śubhāḥ uṣṇasya uṣṇaḥ smṛtaḥ deśaḥ pīvarasya api pīvaraḥ ete janapadāḥ sapta krauñcadvīpe tu bhāsvarāḥ udbhidaḥ veṇumān ca eva svairathaḥ lavaṇaḥ dhṛtiḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ prabhākaraḥ ca eva saptamaḥ kapilaḥ smṛtaḥ udbhidam prathamam varṣam dvitīyam veṇumaṇḍalam tṛtīyam svairathākāram caturtham lavaṇam smṛtam pañcamam dhṛtimat varṣam ṣaṣṭham varṣam prabhākaram teṣām dvīpāḥ kuśadvīpe tad sanāmānaḥ eva tu āśrama ācāra yuktābhiḥ prajābhiḥ samalaṃkṛtāḥ śālmalasya īśvarāḥ sapta putrāḥ te tu vapuṣmataḥ śvetaḥ ca haritaḥ ca eva jīmūtaḥ rohitaḥ tathā jīmūtasya ca jīmūtaḥ haritasya ca hāritaḥ saptadvīpe tu vakṣyāmi jambūdvīpāt anantaram sapta medhātitheḥ putrāḥ plakṣadvīpa īśvarāḥ nṛpāḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ śāntabhayaḥ teṣām sapta varṣāṇi tāni vai ānandaḥ ca dhruvaḥ ca eva kṣemakaḥ ca śivaḥ tathā tāni teṣām sanāmāni sapta varṣāṇi bhāgaśas varṇa āśrama ācāra yuktāḥ plakṣadvīpe prajāḥ kṛtāḥ plakṣadvīpa ādikeṣu eva śākadvīpa antareṣu vai jñeyaḥ pañcasu dharmaḥ vai varṇa āśrama vibhāgaśaḥ sukham āyuḥ ca rūpam ca balam dharmaḥ ca nityaśas pañcasu eteṣu dvīpeṣu sarvam sādhāraṇam smṛtam āgnīdhram jyeṣṭha dāyādam kanyā putram mahā balam priyavrataḥ abhyaṣiñcat tam jambūdvīpa īśvaram nṛpam harivarṣaḥ tṛtīyaḥ tu caturthaḥ abhūt ilāvṛtaḥ ramyaḥ syāt pañcamaḥ putraḥ harinmān ṣaṣṭhaḥ ucyate kuruḥ tu saptamaḥ teṣām bhadrāśvaḥ hi aṣṭamaḥ smṛtaḥ navamaḥ ketumālaḥ tu teṣām deśān nibodhata nābheḥ tu dakṣiṇam varṣam himādvantu pitā dadau hema kūṭam tu yat varṣam dadau kimpuruṣāya tat naiṣadham yat smṛtam varṣam harivarṣāya tat dadau yat smṛtam varṣam ramyāya etat pitā dadau varṣam mālyavataḥ śca api bhadrāśvāya nyavedayat iti etāni mahānti iha nava varṣāṇi bhāgaśas āgnīdhraḥ teṣu sarveṣu putrān tān abhyaṣiñcata iti etaiḥ sapbhiḥ kṛtsnāḥ sapta dvīpāḥ niveśitāḥ yāni kimpuruṣa ādyāni varṣāṇi aṣṭau śubhāni tu teṣām svabhāvataḥ siddhiḥ sukha prāyā hi ayatnataḥ dharma adharmau na teṣu āstām na uttama adhama madhyamāḥ na teṣu asti yuga avasthā kṣetreṣu eva tu sarvaśas nābhiḥ tu ajanayat putram meऱudevyām mahā dyutiḥ ṛṣabham pārthiva śreṣṭham sarva kṣatrasya pūrvajam ṛṣabhāt bharataḥ jajñe vīraḥ putra śata agrajaḥ saḥ abhiṣicya atha bharataḥ putram prāvrājyam āsthitaḥ himāhvam dakṣiṇam varṣam bharatāya nyavedayat tasmāt tat bhāratam varṣam tasya nāmnā viduḥ budhāḥ putra saṃkrāmita śrīkaḥ vanam rājā viveśa saḥ parameṣṭī sutaḥ ca atha nidhane tasya śobhanaḥ pratīhāra kule tasya nāmnā jajñe tad anvayāt pṛthoḥ ca api sutaḥ naktaḥ naktasya api gayaḥ smṛtaḥ virāj sutaḥ mahā vīryaḥ dīmān tasya sutaḥ abhavat dhīmataḥ ca mahān putraḥ mahataḥ ca api bhauvanaḥ tasya putra śatam tu āsīt rājānaḥ sarve eva te viśvajyotiḥ pradhānāyaiḥ taiḥ imāḥ varddhitāḥ prajāḥ taiḥ idam bhāratam varṣam sapta khaṇḍam kṛtam purā teṣām vaṃśa prakūtaiḥ tu bhuktā iyam bhāratī dharā kṛta tretā ādi yuktāni yuga ākhyāni ekasaptatiḥ ye atītāḥ taiḥ yugaiḥ sārddham rājānaḥ te tad anvayāḥ svāyambhuve antare pūrvam śataśas atha sahasraśas eṣa svāyambhuvaḥ sargaḥ yena idam pūritam jagat ṛṣibhiḥ daivataiḥ ca api pitṛ gandharva rākṣasaiḥ yakṣa bhūta piśācaiḥ ca manuṣya mṛga pakṣibhiḥ taiṣām sṛṣṭiḥ iyam loke yugaiḥ saha vivarttate iti śrī mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte svāyambhuva vaṃśānukīrttanam nāma trayastriśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ evam prajā sanniveśam śrutvā ca ṛṣi puṅgavaḥ papraccha nipuṇaḥ sūtam pṛthivī āyāma vistarau kati dvīpāḥ samudrāḥ vā parvatāḥ ca kati prabhoḥ kiyanti ca eva varṣāṇi teṣu nadyaḥ ca kāḥ smṛtāḥ mahābhūta pramāṇam ca lokāḥ lokau tathā eva ca gatiḥ candra arkayoḥ tathā etat prabrūhi naḥ sarvam vistareṇa yathā tathā uvāca atas ūrddhvam pravakṣyāmi pṛthivyāyāma vistaram saṅkhyāḥ ca eva samudrāṇām dvīpānām ca eva vistaram yāvanti ca eva varṣāṇi teṣu nadyaḥ ca yāḥ smṛtāḥ mahābhūta pramāṇam ca loka alokau tathā eva ca gatiḥ candra arkayoḥ tathā na śakyante pramāṇena vaktum varṣa śataiḥ api yeṣām manuṣyāḥ tarkeṇa pramāṇāni pracakṣate acintyāḥ khalu ye bhāvāḥ na tān tarkeṇa bhāvayet nava varṣam pravakṣyāmi jambūdvīpam yathā tathā śatam ekam sahasrāṇām yojanānām pramāṇataḥ nānā janapada ākīrṇaiḥ puraiḥ ca vividhaiḥ śubhaiḥ jambūdvīpaḥ pṛthuḥ śrīmān sarvvatas parivāritaḥ navabhiḥ ca āvṛtaḥ sarvvaiḥ bhuvanaiḥ bhūtabhāvanaiḥ lāvaṇena samudreṇa sarvvatas parivāritaḥ prāc āyatāḥ su parvāṇaḥ ṣaṭ ime varṣaparvatāḥ avagāḍhāḥ ubhayatas samudrau pūrva paśu imau hima prāyaḥ ca himavān hemakūṭaḥ ca hemavān taruṇa āditya varṇa ābhaḥ hairaṇyaḥ niṣadhaḥ smṛtaḥ cāturvarṇaḥ tu sauvarṇaḥ meruḥ ca ucyatamaḥ smṛtaḥ pluta ākṛti pramāṇaḥ ca catur asraḥ samucchritaḥ nānā varṇaḥ tu pārśveṣu prajāpati guṇa anvitaḥ pītaḥ ca dakṣiṇena asau tena vaiśya tvam iṣyate bhṛṅga patra nibha śvāsau pakṣu imena mahā balaḥ tena asya śūdra tā dṛṣṭā meroḥ nānā artha kāraṇāt tena asya kṣatra tā ca syāt iti varṇāḥ prakīrtitāḥ vyaktaḥ svabhāvataḥ proktaḥ varṇataḥ parimāṇataḥ nīlaḥ ca vaiḍhūryya mayaḥ śveta śrṛṅgaḥ hiraṇmayaḥ mayūra barha varṇaḥ tu śātakaumbhaḥ tu śrṛṅgavān ete parvvata rājānaḥ siddha cāraṇa sevitāḥ madhye tu ilāvṛtam yaḥ tu mahāmeroḥ samantataḥ varṣāṇi yāni sapta atra teṣām ye varṣaparvvatāḥ jambūdvīpasya vistārāt teṣām āyāmaḥ ucyate yojanānām sahasrāṇi śate dve madhyamau girī nīlaḥ ca niṣadhaḥ ca eva tābhyām hīnāḥ tu ye apare śvetaḥ ca hemakūṭaḥ ca himavān śrṛṅgavān ca yaḥ navatiḥ dvi iva aśītiḥ dvau sahasrāṇi āyatāḥ tu ye teṣām madhye janapadāḥ tāni varṣāṇi sapta vai vasanti teṣu satvāni nānā jātīni bhāgaśas idam haimavatam varṣam bhāratam nāma viśrutam hemakūṭam param tasmāt nāmnā kimpuruṣam smṛtam naiṣadham hemakūṭam tu harivarṣam tat ucyate harivarṣāt param ca eva meroḥ ca tat ilāvṛtam ilāvṛta param nīlam ramyakam nāma viśrutam hiraṇmayāt param ca api śrṛṅgavān tu kuru smṛtam dīrghāṇi tatra catvāri madhyamantat ilāvṛtam arvāk ca niṣadhasya atha vedyarddham dakṣiṇam smṛtam vedi arddham dakṣiṇe trīṇi varṣāṇi trīṇi ca uttare udak āyataḥ mahā śailaḥ mālyavān nāma parvvataḥ yojanānām sahasra ūruḥ ā nīla niṣadha āyataḥ prakīrtitaḥ tasya pratīcyām vijñeyaḥ parvataḥ gandhamādanaḥ āyāmāt atha vistārāt mālyavān iti viśrutaḥ avyaktāḥ dhātavaḥ sarvve samutpannāḥ jala ādayaḥ catuṣpatham samutpannam vyaktam pañcaguṇam mahat tatas sarvvāḥ samutpannāḥ vṛttayaḥ dvijasattamāḥ kṛtātmabhiḥ vinīta ātmā mahātmā puruṣottamaḥ na tasya prākṛtī mūrttiḥ māṃsa medaḥ asthi sambhavā yogāt ca eva īśvara tvāt ca sarvva ātmā āgataḥ eva saḥ kalpa śeṣasya tasya ādau kālasya gatiḥ īdṛśī prajāpati patiḥ brahmā īśānaḥ jagataḥ prabhuḥ yat abjam vaiṣṇavam kāryyam tatas tat nābhitaḥ abhavat padma ākārā samutpannā pṛthivī sa vana drumā varṇa mānam vibhāgena kramaśas śrṛṇuta dvijāḥ mahā dvīpāḥ tu vikhyātāḥ catvāraḥ pattra saṃsthitāḥ tatas karṇika saṃsthānaḥ meruḥ nāma mahā balaḥ nānā varṇeṣu pārśveṣu pūrvatas śvetaḥ ucyate pītantu dakṣiṇam tasya śṛṅgam kṛṣṇam tathā aparam meruḥ tu śobhate śubhraḥ rāja vat sa tu dhiṣṭitaḥ taruṇa āditya varṇa ābhaḥ vidhūmaḥ iva pāvakaḥ praviṣṭaḥ ṣoḍaśa adhastāt vistṛtaḥ tāvat eva tu sa śara avasthitaḥ pūrvam dvātriṃśat mūrdhni vistṛtaḥ vistārāt triguṇaḥ ca asya pariṇāhaḥ samantataḥ catvāriṃśat sahasrāṇi yojanānām samantataḥ catur asreṇa mānena pariṇāhaḥ samantataḥ catuḥṣaṣṭi sahasrāṇi yojanānām vidhīyate bhuvanaiḥ āvṛtaḥ sarvaḥ jātarūpa mayaiḥ śubhaiḥ tatra deva gaṇāḥ sarve gandharva uraga rākṣasāḥ śailarājaiḥ pradṛśyante śubhāḥ ca apsarasā aṅgaṇāḥ catvāraḥ yasya deśāḥ vai nānā pārśveṣu adhiṣṭitāḥ bhadrāśvaḥ bharataḥ ca eva ketumālaḥ ca paścimaḥ uttarāḥ kuravaḥ ca eva kṛta puṇya pratiśrayāḥ karṇikā tasya padmasya samantāt parimaṇḍalā yojanānām sahasrāṇi navatiḥ ṣaḍ prakīrttitāḥ catvāraḥ ca api aśītiḥ ca antara antara dhiṣṭitāḥ tri śatam ca sahasrāṇi yojanānām pramāṇataḥ tasya keśara jālāni vistīrṇāni samantataḥ śata sāhasrika āyāmā sa aśīti pṛthulā āyatā catvāri tasya patrāṇi yojanānām caturddiśam tatra yā asau mayā pūrvam karṇikā iti abhiśabditā tām varṇyamānām ekāgrāḥ samāsena nibodhata śata aśrim enam mene atriḥ sahasra aśrim ṛṣiḥ bhṛguḥ aṣṭa aśrim enam sāvarṇiḥ catur asran tu bhāguriḥ vārṣāyaṇiḥ tu sāmudram śarāvan ca eva gālavaḥ ūrddhvaveṇīkṛtam gārgyaḥ kroṣṭakiḥ parimaṇḍalam maṇi ratna mayam citram nānā varṇa prabhā yutam suvarṇa maṇi citra aṅgam tathā vidruma toraṇaiḥ vimāna yānaiḥ śrīmadbhiḥ śata saṅkhyaiḥ divaukasām prabhā dīpita paryantam merum parvaṇi parvaṇi sarva deva nikāyāni sanniviṣṭāni anekaśas brahmā brahma vidām śreṣṭaḥ variṣṭhaḥ tridivaukasām mahā bhuvana sampūrṇaiḥ sarvvaiḥ kāma phala pradaiḥ nāmnā manovatī nāma sarva lokeṣu viśrutā mahā vimānam saṃsthāpya mahimnā vartate sadā tatra sa ṛṣi gaṇāḥ devāḥ caturvaktrasya te tadā tat eva tejasām rāśiḥ devānām tatra kīrttyate tatra āste śrīpatiḥ śrīmān sahasrākṣaḥ purandaraḥ upāsyamānaḥ tridaśaiḥ mahā yogaiḥ sura ṛṣibhiḥ dvitīye api antara taṭe vaidiśye pūrvva dakṣiṇe nānā dhātu śatas citraiḥ su ramyam ati tejasam jāmbūnada kṛta udyānam nānā ratna su vedikam mahā vimānam prathitam bhāskaram jātavedasam sā hi tejovatī nāma hutāśasya mahā sabhā sākṣāt tatra suraśreṣṭhaḥ sarva deva mukhaḥ analaḥ śikhā śata sahasra āḍhyaḥ jvālā mālī vibhāḥ vasuḥ stūyate hūyate ca eva tatra sa ṛṣi gaṇaiḥ suraiḥ sa vibhāgam ca tejaḥ ca sarvaḥ eva na saṃśayaḥ pṛthak tvam ca hi yuktyā tu kārya kāraṇa miśritam vaivasvatasya vijñeyā loke khyātā su saṃyamā nāmnā kṛṣṇā aṅganā nāma virūpākṣasya dhīmataḥ vaivasvatasya vijñeyā nāmnā śubhavatī satī udaka adhipateḥ khyātā varuṇasya mahātmanaḥ para uttare tathā deśe ṣaṣṭe antara taṭe śive vāyoḥ gandhavatī nāma sabhā sarva guṇa uttarā nāmnā mahodayā nāma śuddha vaiḍhūryya vedikā tathā aṣṭame antara taṭe īśānasya mahātmana ᥤ। sūtaḥ uvāca tat yojana sahasrāṇām saptatīnām adhas smṛtam catvariṃśat tathā aṣṭau ca sahasrāṇi atra maṇḍalam śailarāja āvṛtam ramyam meru mūlam iti śrutiḥ teṣām giri sahasrāṇām anekeṣu mahā ucchritāḥ dikṣu sarvāsu paryyantaiḥ maryyādāḥ parvatāḥ smṛtāḥ nikuñja kandara nadī guhā nirjhara śobhitāḥ nitamba puṣpa mālā oghaiḥ sānubhiḥ dhātu maṇḍitaiḥ vihaṅga śata saṃjuṣṭaiḥ kuñjaiḥ anupamaiḥ api siha śārdūla śarabhaiḥ na ekaiḥ ca amara vāraṇaiḥ nānā varṇa ākṛti dharaiḥ sevitāḥ vividhaiḥ nagaiḥ sapta aḥ ca hari kṛṣṇa aṅgam ekaikam daśa parvatam bāhyam ābhyantarāḥ ye tu tri vāhāḥ tu samāḥ smṛtāḥ jaṭharaḥ devakūṭaḥ ca pūrvasyām diśi parvatau tau dakṣiṇa uttara āyāmau ā nīla niṣadha āyatau kailāsaḥ himavān ca eva dakṣiṇa uttara parvatau pūrva paśca āyatau etau arṇava anta vyavasthitau yaḥ asau meruḥ dvijaśreṣṭāḥ prāṃśuḥ kanakaparvataḥ viṣkambham tasya vakṣyāmi tat me nigadataḥ śrṛṇu daśa yojana sāhasraḥ āyāmaḥ teṣu paṭyate deva gandharva yakṣāṇām nānā ratna upaśobhitāḥ nitamba puṣpa kādambaiḥ śobhitāḥ citra sānavaḥ manaḥśilā darībhiḥ ca haritāla talaiḥ tathā suvarṇa maṇi citrābhiḥ guhābhiḥ ca samantataḥ śuddha hiṅgulaka prakhyaiḥ kāñcanaiḥ dhātu maṇḍitaiḥ vara kāñcana citraiḥ ca pravālaiḥ samalaṃkṛtāḥ rucirāḥ śata parvāṇaḥ siddha āvāsāḥ mudā anvitāḥ mahā vimānaiḥ śrīmadbhiḥ samantāt paridīpitāḥ pūrveṇa mandaraḥ nāma dakṣiṇe gandhamādanaḥ vipulaḥ paścime pārśve supārśvaḥ ca uttare smṛtaḥ teṣām sahasra śrṛṅgeṣu vajra vaiḍhūrya vedikāḥ śākhā sahasra kalitāḥ su mūlāḥ su pratiṣṭitāḥ srigdhaiḥ nīlaiḥ ghanaiḥ parṇaiḥ sañjhanna vividha āśrayāḥ yakṣa gandharva sevyāḥ ca sevitāḥ siddha cāraṇaiḥ mahā vṛkṣāḥ samutpannāḥ catvāraḥ dvīpa ketavaḥ mandarasya mahā vṛkṣaḥ sa ketu rāj ālamba śākhā śikharaḥ kandaraḥ ca pādapaḥ mahā gandhaiḥ manojñaiḥ ca śobhitaḥ sarva kāla jaiḥ yojanānām samantāt vai manda māruta vījitaḥ yatra sākṣāt hṛṣīkeśaḥ siddha saṅghaiḥ mahīyate prāptavān apara śreṣṭhaḥ sa tatra sahitaḥ purā tena ca ālokitam sarvam dvīpam dvipada nāyakāḥ yasya nāmnā samākhyātaḥ bhadrāśvaḥ nāma nāmataḥ dakṣiṇasya api śailasya śikhare deva sevitā jambūḥ sadā puṣpa phalā sadā mālya upaśobhitā mahā mūlaiḥ mahā skandhaiḥ snigdha varṇaiḥ vibhūṣitā navaiḥ sadā puṣpa phalaiḥ śākhābhiḥ ca upaśobhitā tasyāḥ hi atipramāṇāni svādūni ca mṛdūni ca nadī jambūnadī nāma pravṛttā madhu vāhinī deva alaṅkāram atulam jāyate pāpa nāśanam deva dānava gandharvāḥ yakṣa rākṣasa pannagāḥ sa ketuḥ dakṣiṇe dvīpe jambhūḥ lokeṣu viśrutā yasyāḥ nāmnā sa vikhyātaḥ jambhūdvīpaḥ sanātanaḥ jātaḥ śrṛṅge ati su mahān aśvatthaḥ ca eva pādapaḥ kumbha pramāṇaiḥ sukha daiḥ phalaiḥ sarva ṛttukaiḥ śubhaiḥ sa ketuḥ ketumālānām deva gandharva sevitaḥ sahasrākṣeṇa vihitā mālā tasya sā tathā eva mahāgandhā hi amlānā sarvakāmikī ijyate su mahābhāgā vividhaiḥ siddha cāraṇaiḥ tasya ketoḥ sadā mālā deva dattā virājate tābhyām nāma aṅkitaḥ dvīpaḥ paścime bahu vistaraḥ sva pārśvasya uttare ca api śrṛṅge jātaḥ mahā drumaḥ mālya dāma kalāpaiḥ ca vividhaiḥ gandha śālibhiḥ śāka avilambī śuśubhe siddha cāraṇa sevitaḥ pravāla kumbha sadṛśaiḥ madhu pūrṇaiḥ phalaiḥ sadā sa hi uttara kurūṇām tu ketu vṛkṣaḥ prakāśate sanatkumāra avarajāḥ mānasāḥ brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ sapta tatra mahābhāgāḥ kuravaḥ nāma viśrutāḥ tatra taiḥ āgata jñānaiḥ sattva sthaiḥ puṇya kīrtibhiḥ akṣayam kṣemam aparam lokam prāptam sanātanam teṣām nāma aṅkitaḥ dvīpaḥ saptānām vai mahātmanām divi ca iha ca vikhyātāḥ uttarāḥ kuravaḥ sadā iti śrī mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte jambūdvīpavarṇanam nāma pañcatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca teṣām caturṇām vakṣyāmi śailendrāṇām yathākramam sārikābhiḥ mayūraiḥ ca cakoraiḥ ca mada utkaṭaiḥ śukaiḥ ca bhṛṅgarājaiḥ ca citrakaiḥ ca samantataḥ jīvañjīvaka nādaiḥ ca hemakānām ca nāditaiḥ matta kokila nādaiḥ ca valgūnām ca nināditaiḥ sugrīva kāñcana ravaiḥ kalaviṅka rutaiḥ tathā kūjita antara śabdaiḥ ca su ramyāṇi ca sarvaśas puṣpa vṛṣṭim vimuñcanti manda māruta kampitāḥ taravaḥ yatra dṛśyante cāru pallava śobhitāḥ nānā dhātu vicitraiḥ ca kānta rūpaiḥ śilā śataiḥ śallaiḥ vkacid dvijaśreṣṭāḥ vinyastaiḥ śobhitāni ca manoharāṇi catvāri deva ākrīḍanakāni atha caturdiśam udārāṇi nāmnā śrṛṇuta tāni me pūrvañcaitraratham nāma dakṣiṇam nandanam vanam mahā vaneṣu ca eteṣu niviṣṭāni yathākramam anubandhāni ramyāṇi vihaṅgaiḥ kūjitāni ca vanaiḥ vistīrṇa tīrthāni mahā puṇya vanāni ca mahā nāga adhivāsāni sevitāni mahātmabhiḥ śivāni su sukhāni ca puṇḍarīkaiḥ mahā patraiḥ utpalaiḥ śobhitāni ca mahāsarāṃsi catvāri tāni vakṣyāmi nāmataḥ aruṇodam saraḥ pūrvam dakṣiṇam mānasam smṛtam pūrveṇa ye ca śailāḥ tatas smṛtāḥ tān kīrtyamānān tattvena śrṛṇudhvam vistarān mama śītāntaḥ ca kumuñjaḥ ca suvīraḥ ca acala uttamaḥ vikaṅkaḥ maṇiśīlaḥ ca vṛṣabhaḥ ca acala uttamaḥ veṇumān ca sumedhaḥ ca niṣadhaḥ deva parvataḥ pūrveṇa mandarasya ete siddha vāsāḥ udāhṛtāḥ sarasaḥ mānasasya iha dakṣiṇāḥ ye mahā acalāḥ śailaḥ tri śikharaḥ ca api śiśiraḥ ca acala uttamaḥ kaliṅgaḥ ca pataṅgaḥ ca rucakaḥ ca eva sānumān tāmra ābhaḥ ca viśākhaḥ ca tathā śvetodaraḥ giriḥ sa mūlaḥ viṣa dhāraḥ ca ratna dhāraḥ ca parvataḥ pañcaśailaḥ atha kailāsaḥ himavant ca acala uttamaḥ iti ete deva caritāḥ hi utkṛṣṭāḥ parvata uttamāḥ uttamāḥ ye mahā śailāḥ tān pravakṣye yathākramam suvakṣāḥ śikhiśailaḥ ca kālaḥ vaiḍhūrya parvataḥ kapilaḥ piṅgalaḥ rudraḥ surasaḥ ca mahā acalaḥ kumudaḥ madhumān ca eva añjanīmukuṭaḥ tathā kṛṣṇaḥ ca pāṇḍaraḥ ca eva sahasraśikharaḥ ca ha pāriyātraḥ ca śaila indraḥ triśrṛṅgaḥ ca acala uttamaḥ iti ete parvata varāḥ digbhāge paścime smṛtāḥ mahābhadrasya sarasaḥ uttareṇa api śrīmataḥ ye mayā pūrvatas proktāḥ tān vadiṣye yathākramam śaṅkukūṭaḥ mahā śailaḥ vṛṣabhaḥ haṃsaparvataḥ nāgaḥ ca kapilaḥ ca eva indraśailaḥ ca sānumān nīlaḥ kanaka śrṛṅgaḥ ca śataśrṛṅgaḥ ca parvataḥ puṣpakaḥ meghaśailaḥ ca virājaḥ ca acala uttamaḥ jārudhiḥ ca eva śailendraḥ iti ete uttarāḥ smṛtāḥ eteṣām śaila mukhyānām antareṣu yathākramam iti śrī mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte bhuvanavinyāsaḥ nāma ṣaṭtriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca śīta antasya acala indrasya kumuñjasya antareṇa tu droṇyaḥ vihaṅga saṅghuṣṭāḥ nānā sattva niṣevitāḥ tri yojana śata āyāmāḥ vistīrṇāḥ śata yojanāḥ droṇyāyāma pramāṇaiḥ tu puṇḍarīkaiḥ sugandhibhiḥ deva dānava gandharvaiḥ upaspṛṣṭam jalam śubham puṇyam tat śrīsaraḥ nāma prakāśam divi ca iha ca prasanna jala sampūrṇam śaraṇyam sarva dehinām nityam vyākośam ajaram cāñcalyāt ca ati maṇḍalam cāru keśara jāla āḍhyam matta ṣaṭpada nāditam lakṣmyāḥ padmam tadā āvāsam mūrttimatyāḥ na saṃśayaḥ śata yojana vistīrṇam tri yojana śatāya tam ardha krośa ucca śikharaiḥ mahā vṛkṣaiḥ sahasraśas phalaiḥ suvarṇa saṅkāśaiḥ haritaiḥ pāṇḍaraiḥ tathā amṛta svādu sadṛśaiḥ bherī mātraiḥ sugandhibhiḥ śīryamāṇaiḥ patadbhiḥ ca kīrṇā bhūmiḥ nirantarā nāmnā tat śrīvanam nāma sarva lokeṣu viśrutam siddhaiḥ ca eva samākīrṇam nityam bilva phala āśibhiḥ śata yojana vistīrṇam dvi yojana śata āyatam puṣpa lakṣmyā āvṛtam bhāti jvalantam iva nityadā arddha krośa ucca śikharaiḥ mahā skandhaiḥ palāśibhiḥ praphulla śākhā śikharaiḥ piñjaram bhāti tat vanam manaḥ śilā cūrṇa nibhaiḥ pāṇḍu kesara śālibhiḥ puṣpaiḥ manoharaiḥ vyāptam vyākośaiḥ gandha śālibhiḥ tatra āśramam bhagavataḥ kaśyapasya prajāpateḥ siddha sādhya gaṇā kīrṇam nānā śruti vibhūṣitam mahānīla kumuñjābhyām antare pi acalau atha mahānadyāḥ sukhāyāḥ tu tīre siddha niṣevite pañcāśat yojana āyāmam triṃśat yojana vistaram mahā mūlaiḥ mahā sāraiḥ sthiraiḥ aviralaiḥ śubhaiḥ kumuda añjana saṃsthānaiḥ parivṛttaiḥ mahā phalaiḥ sahasra yojana āyāmam vistīrṇam śata yojanam sahasra yojana āyāmā śata yojana vistṛtā sa vāṃhi eka śilā bhūmiḥ vṛkṣa vīrudh vivarjitā āplutā pāda mātreṇa hi udakena samantataḥ iti etāḥ hi antara droṇyaḥ nānā ākārāḥ prakīrttitāḥ meroḥ pūrveṇa vipra indrāḥ yathāvat anupūrvaśas iti śrī mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte bhuvanavinyāsaḥ nāma saptatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca atas param pravakṣyāmi dakṣiṇān diśam āśritāḥ yāḥ droṇyaḥ siddha caritāḥ śṛṇu tāḥ hi anupūrvaśas śiśirasya acala indrasya pataṅgasya antareṇa ca ślakṣṇa bhūmi śriyā yuktam latā āliṅgita pādapam vidyādharāḥ ca muditāḥ upajīvanti nityaśas surasa amala toyāḥ tāḥ sarāṃsi ca samantataḥ ramyam sura gaṇa ākīrṇam sarvatas citra kānanam samantāt yojana śatam tat vanam parimaṇḍalam tāmra varṇasya śailasya pataṅgasya antareṇa tu śata yojana vistīrṇam dvi yojana śata āyatam taruṇa āditya saṅkāśaiḥ puṇḍarīkaiḥ samantataḥ tathā bhramara saṃlīnaiḥ śatapatraiḥ sugandhibhiḥ mahā uragaiḥ adhyuṣitam nīla jāla vibhūṣitam triṃśat yojana vistīrṇaḥ rakta dhātu vibhūṣitaḥ tasya upari mahā ramyā prāṃśu prākāra toraṇā nara nārī gaṇa ākīrṇā sphītā vibhava vistaraiḥ mahā bhavana mālābhiḥ mahā prāṃśubhiḥ uttamaiḥ citra veṣa dharaḥ sragvī māhendra sadṛśa dyutiḥ dīptānām citra veṣāṇām sūrya pratima tejasām vidyādhara sahasrāṇām anekeṣām sa rāja rāj viśākhasya acala indrasya pataṅgasya antareṇa ca pañca iṣu kṣepaṇaiḥ viddham su śākham varṇa śobhitam kāla phalam tatra sphītam ca āmravaṇam mahat phalaiḥ kanaka saṅkāśaiḥ mahā āsvādaiḥ sugandhibhiḥ mahā kumbha pramāṇaiḥ ca a tanu śākhaiḥ samantataḥ gandharva kinnarāḥ yakṣāḥ nāgāḥ vidyādharāḥ tathā tatra āmra rasa pītānām muditānām mahātmanām śrūyante hṛṣṭa puṣṭānām nādāḥ tasmin mahā vane samā surabhi pūrṇa āḍhyā vihaṅgaiḥ upaśobhitā triṃśat yojana vistīrṇā pañcāśat yojana āyatā tatra bilva sthalī viprāḥ śuddhāḥ nimna phala drumāḥ śīryamāṇaiḥ viśīrṇaiḥ ca praklinna tala mṛttikāḥ tām sthalīm upajīvanti yakṣa gandharva kinnarāḥ siddhāḥ nāgāḥ ca bahuśas nityam bilva phala āśinaḥ triṃśat yojana vistīrṇam āyatam śata yojanam sugandham kiṃśuka vanam nityam puṣpita pādapam puṣpa lakṣmyā āvṛtam bhāti pradīptam iva sarvatas samagram yojana śatam kānanāni samantataḥ ramyam tat kiṃśuka vanam jalāśaya vibhūṣitam māse māse anatarati tatra sūryaḥ prajāpatiḥ tatra kālasya karttāram sahasrāṃśum sura uttamam pañcakūṭasya śailasya kailāsasya antareṇa tu ṣaṭtriṃśat yojana āyāmam vistīrṇam śata yojanam kṣudra sattvaiḥ anādhṛṣyam sarvatas haṃsa pāṇḍuram duṣpāram sarva satvānām durgamam loma harṣaṇam iti etāḥ hi antara droṇyaḥ dakṣiṇe parikīrtitāḥ yathānupūrvam akhilāḥ siddha saṅgha niṣevitāḥ paśu imāyām diśi tathā ye antara droṇi vistarāḥ tān varṇyamānān tatvena śrṛṇuta imān dvijottamāḥ antarāle girau tasmin su vakṣaḥ śikhi śailayoḥ samantāt yojana śatam eka bhūmam śilā talam nitya taptam mahā ghoram duḥsparśam roma harṣaṇam agamyam sarva sattvānām īśvarāṇām su dāruṇam madhye tasyām śilā sthalyām triṃśat yojana maṇḍalam jvālā sahasra kalilam vahni sthānam su dāruṇam an indhanaḥ tatra sadā jvālā mālī vibhāvasuḥ jvalati eṣa sadā devaḥ śaśvat tatra hutāśanaḥ antare śaila varayoḥ devāḥ vā api tayoḥ śubhāḥ mātuluṅga sthalī tatra hi āyāmāt daśa yojanā phalaiḥ pariṇataiḥ sarvā śobhitā sā mahā sthalī tatra āśramam mahā puṇyam siddha saṅgha niṣevitam candra aṃśu varṇaiḥ vyākośaiḥ matta ṣaṭpada nāditaiḥ śabalam tat vanam bhāti kusumaiḥ sarva kāla jaiḥ tatra viṣṇoḥ suraguroḥ dīptam āyatanam mahat antare śaila varayoḥ kṛṣṇa pāṇḍurayoḥ api triṃśat yojana vistīrṇam navati āyata yojanam ślakṣṇam eka śilam deśam vṛkṣa vīrudh vivarjitam sahasra patraiḥ vyākośaiḥ chatra mātraiḥ alaṅkṛtā puṇḍarīkaiḥ mahā padmaiḥ ruciraiḥ gandha śālibhiḥ mṛdu gadghada kaṇṭānām kinnarāṇām nisvanaiḥ upagīta padma khaṇḍa āḍhyā vistīrṇā sthalapadminī madhye tasyāḥ ca padminyāḥ pañca yojana maṇḍalaḥ tatra candra prabhaḥ śrīmān pūrṇa candra nibha ānana sahasra vadanaḥ devaḥ nīla vāsāḥ surāri hā padma mālya dhara sthalyām mahābhāgaḥ aparājitaḥ tasmin āyatane sākṣāt anādinidhanaḥ hariḥ padma mālā avalambābhiḥ mālābhiḥ upaśobhitam pañcāśat yojana āyāmam triṃśat yojana vistaram iṣu kṣepa ucca śikharam nānā vihaga sevitam tatra āśramam mahā puṇyam deva ṛṣi gaṇa sevitam śukrasya prathitam tatra bhāsvaram puṇya karmaṇaḥ śaṅkukūṭasya śailasya vṛṣabhasya antareṇa ca parūṣaka sthalī ramyā hi aneka āyata yojanā bilva pramāṇaiḥ ca śubhaiḥ mahā svādaiḥ sugandhibhiḥ tām sthalīm upajīvanti kinnara uraga sādhavaḥ parūṣaka rasa unmattāḥ māna āḍhyāḥ tatra cāraṇāḥ dvi yojana śata āyāmā vistīrṇā śata yojanā sthalī manoharā sā hi nānā vana vibhūṣitā drākṣā vanāni ramyāṇi tathā nāga vanāni ca kharjūra vana khaṇḍāni nīla aśoka vanāni ca dāḍimānām ca svādūnām akṣoṭaka vanāni ca atasī tilakānām ca kadalīnām vanāni ca badarīṇām ca svādūnām vana khaṇḍāni sarvaśas svādu śīta ambu pūrṇābhiḥ nadībhiḥ śobhitāni ca ṣaṣṭi yojana vistīrṇā sā bhūmiḥ śatam āyatā samā pāṇi tala prakhyā kaṭinā pāṇḍurā ghanā vṛkṣa gulma latā gulmaiḥ tṛṇaiḥ ca api vivarjitā sā kānanasthalī nāma dāruṇā romaharṣaṇā mahā sarāṃsi ca tathā mahā vṛkṣāḥ tathā eva ca mahā vanāni sarvāṇi kānta nāmāni sarvaśas sarasām ca vanānām ca sā sthalī ca prajāpateḥ kṣudrāṇām sarasām ca eva saṅkhyā tatra na vidyate daśa dvādaśa sapta aṣṭau viṃśatrriṃśat ca yojanāḥ sthalyaḥ droṇyaḥ ca vikhyātāḥ sarāṃsi ca vanāni ca kecid santi mahā ghorāḥ śyāmāḥ parvata kukṣayaḥ sūrya aṃśu jālaiḥ a spṛṣṭāḥ nityam śītāḥ durāsadāḥ tathā hi anala taptāni sarāṃsi dvijasattamāḥ śaila kukṣi antara sthāni sahasrāṇi śatāni ca iti śrī mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte bhuvanavinyāsaḥ nāma aṣṭatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca ye sanniviṣṭāḥ devānām vividhānām gṛha uttamāḥ tatra yaḥ asau mahā śailaḥ śīta antaḥ na eka vistaraḥ mahārha maṇi citrābhiḥ hema vaṃśaiḥ alaṃkṛtaḥ nitambaiḥ ṣaṭpada udgītaiḥ pravālaiḥ hema citrakaiḥ taṭaiḥ kusuma saṅkīrṇaiḥ matta bhramara nāditaiḥ latā ālambaiḥ citravadbhiḥ citraiḥ dhātu śata arcitaiḥ sānubhiḥ ratna citraiḥ ca puṣpa āḍhyaiḥ ca vibhūṣitaḥ nikuñjaiḥ kusuma utkīrṇaiḥ anekaiḥ ca vibhūṣitaḥ puṣma oḍupa vahābhiḥ ca sravantībhiḥ alaṃkṛtaḥ kinnara ācaritābhiḥ ca darībhiḥ sarvatas tatas śobhitaḥ ca sukha āsevyaiḥ citraiḥ gahana saṅkaṭaiḥ nānā satva gaṇa ākīrṇaiḥ su pānīyaiḥ sukha āśrayaiḥ nānā puṣpa phala upetaiḥ pādapaiḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ prakāśam triṣu lokeṣu gīyate śruti niścayāt taruṇa āditya saṃkāśaiḥ mahā gandhaiḥ manoharaiḥ puṣpaiḥ bhāti naga śreṣṭhaḥ su dīptaḥ iva sarvaśas pārijātaka puṣmāṇām māhendra vana nirgataḥ vaiḍhūrya nīlaiḥ kamalaiḥ sauvarṇaiḥ vajra kesaraiḥ sa paṅkajaiḥ mahā patraiḥ vāpyaḥ tatra vibhūṣitāḥ virejuḥ antar ambu sthāḥ sauvarṇa maṇi bhūṣitāḥ nityam mīna yūthāḥ sahasraśas kūrmaiḥ ca aneka saṃsthānaiḥ hema ratna pariṣkṛtaiḥ cañcūryamāṇaiḥ salilaiḥ bhāti citram samantataḥ nānā varṇaiḥ ca śakhunaiḥ nānā ratna tanūruhaiḥ suvarṇa puṣpaiḥ ca anekaiḥ maṇi tuṇḍaiḥ dvijātibhiḥ śuśubhe tat vanam ramyam sahasrākṣasya dhīmataḥ matta bhramara sat nādaiḥ vihaṅgānām ca kūjitaiḥ nityam ā nanditavanam tasmāt krīḍā vanam mahat suvarṇa pārśvaiḥ ca nagaiḥ maṇi muktā puraskṛtaiḥ maṇi śrṛṅga kalā āpannaiḥ patadbhiḥ ca samantataḥ śākhāmṛgaiḥ ca citra aṅgaiḥ nānā ratna tanūruhaiḥ nānā varṇa prakāraiḥ ca sattvaiḥ anyaiḥ samākulam muñcanti puṣpa varṣam ca tatra bāla latāḥ drumāḥ pārijātaka puṣpāṇām manda māruta kampitāḥ śayana āsana nirvyūhaiḥ stīrṇaiḥ ratna vibhūṣitaiḥ vihāra bhūmayaḥ tatra dvijāḥ śakra vane śubhāḥ na ca śītaḥ na ca api uṣṇaḥ raviḥ tatra samaḥ sadā vāti ca api anilaḥ tatra nānā puṣpa adhivāsitaḥ nityam saṅga sukha āhlādī śrama klama vināśanaḥ yakṣa rākṣasa guhyāḥ ca gandharvāḥ ca amita ojasaḥ vidyādharāḥ ca siddhāḥ ca kinnarāḥ ca mudā yutāḥ atha apsaraḥ gaṇāḥ ca eva nityam krīḍā parāyaṇāḥ tasya dhātu vicitreṣu kūṭeṣu bahu vistarāḥ aṣṭau puryaḥ hi udīrṇāḥ ca dānavānām mahātmanām udīrṇāḥ rākṣasa āvāsāḥ nara nārī samākulāḥ nīlakāḥ nāma te ghorāḥ rākṣasāḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ tatra te abhiratāḥ nityam mahā bala parākramāḥ mahānīle api śaila indre purāṇi daśa pañca ca haya ānanānām vikhyātāḥ kinnarāṇām mahātmanām tatra kinnara rājānaḥ daśa pañca ca garvitāḥ suvarṇa pārśvāḥ prāyeṇa nānā parṇa samākulaiḥ bila praveśaiḥ nagaraiḥ śaila indraḥ saḥ abhyalaṃkṛtaḥ ati dāruṇāḥ dṛṣṭi viṣāḥ hi agni kopāḥ durāsadāḥ sunāge api mahā śaile daitya āvāsā sahasraśas harmya prāsāda kalilāḥ prāṃśu prākāra toraṇāḥ triṃśat ad yojana vistīrṇam pañcāśat yojana āyatam ulūkaḥ romaśaḥ ca eva mahānetraḥ ca vīryavān vidyādhara varāḥ tatra śakra tulya parākramāḥ tatra āste gāruḍiḥ nityam uraga ariḥ durāsadaḥ mahā vāyu javaḥ caṇḍaḥ sugrīvaḥ nāma vīryavān mahā pramāṇaiḥ vikrāntaiḥ mahā bala parākramaiḥ sa śailaḥ hi āvṛtaḥ sarvaḥ pakṣibhiḥ pannaga aribhiḥ karañje abhirataḥ nityam sākṣāt bhūtapatiḥ prabhuḥ vṛṣabhāṅkaḥ mahādevaḥ śaṅkaraḥ yoginām prabhuḥ nānā veṣa dharaiḥ bhūtaiḥ pramathaiḥ ca durāsadaiḥ karañje sānavaḥ sarve hi avakīrṇāḥ samantataḥ vasu dhāre vasumatām vasūnām amita ojasām aṣṭāvāyatanāni āhuḥ pūjitāni mahātmanām ratnadhātau giri vare ṛṣīṇām ca mahātmanām sapta āśramāṇi puṇyāni siddha āvāsa yutāni ca mahāprajāpateḥ sthānam hemaśrṛṅgaḥ naga uttame gajaśaile bhagavataḥ nānā bhūta gaṇa āvṛtāḥ rudrāḥ pramuditāḥ nityam sarva bhūta namaskṛtāḥ ādityānām vasūnām ca rudrāṇām ca amita ojasām tatra āyatana vinyāsāḥ ramyāḥ ca eva aśvinoḥ api sthānāni siddhaiḥ devānām sthāpitāni naga uttame tatra pūjā parāḥ nityam yakṣa gandharva kinnarāḥ aśīti amara purī ābhā mahā prākāra toraṇā siddhāḥ hi apattanāḥ nāma gandharvāḥ yuddha śālinaḥ yeṣām adhipatiḥ devaḥ rājarājaḥ kapiñjalaḥ anale rākṣasa āvāsāḥ pañcakūṭe api dānavāḥ ūrjitāḥ deva ripavaḥ mahā bala parākramāḥ śataśrṛhge pura śatam yakṣāṇām amita ojasām viśākhe parvata śreṣṭe na eka vapra darī śubhe śvetodare mahā śaile mahā bhavana maṇḍite piśācake giri vare harmyam prāsāda maṇḍitam harikūṭe hariḥ devaḥ sarva bhūta namaskṛtaḥ prabhāvāt tasya śailaḥ asau mahānābhaḥ prakāśate kumude kinnarā vāsāḥ añjane ca mahā uragāḥ kṛṣṇe gandharvanagarāḥ mahā bhavana śālinaḥ pāṇḍure cāru śikhare mahā prākāra toraṇe purāṇi samudīrṇānām sahasram hema mālinām mukuṭe pannaga āvāsāḥ anekāḥ parvata uttamāḥ puṣpake vai muni gaṇāḥ nityam eva mudā yutāḥ siddhaiḥ hi teṣu sthāneṣu nityam iṣṭaḥ prapūjyate iti śrī mahā purāṇe vāyuprokte bhuvanavinyāsaḥ nāma ekonacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca samantāt yojana śatam mahā bhavana maṇḍitam na ekaiḥ mahā pakṣi gaṇaiḥ gāruḍaiḥ śīgra vikramaiḥ mahāvāyupraveśasya śālmali dvīpa vāsinaḥ dakṣiṇeṣu vicitreṣu saptasu api tu śobhinaḥ sandhyā abhra ābhāḥ samuditāḥ rukma prākāra toraṇāḥ mahā bhavana mālābhiḥ śobhitāḥ deva nirmitāḥ triṃśat yojana vistīrṇāḥ catvāriṃśattama āyatāḥ sapta gandharvanagarāḥ nara nārī samākulāḥ āgneyāḥ nāma gandharvāḥ mahā bala parākramāḥ kubera anucarāḥ dīptāḥ teṣām te bhavana uttamāḥ puram āśīviṣaiḥ purṇam mahā prākāra toraṇam duṣprasahyam amitrāṇām triṃśat yojana maṇḍalam nagaram saiṃhikeyānām udīrṇam deva vidviṣām dvitīye dvija śārdūla maryyādāparvate śubhe mahā bhavana mālābhiḥ nānā varṇābhiḥ āvṛtam suvarṇa maṇi citrābhiḥ anekābhiḥ alaṃkṛtam viśāla rathyam durdharṣam nityam pramuditam śivam nara nārī gaṇa ākīrṇam prāṃśu prākāra toraṇam ṣaṣṭi yojana vistīrṇam śata yojanam āyatam nagaram kālakeyānām asurāṇām durāsadam devakūṭa taṭe ramye sanniviṣṭam su durjayam mahā abhra caya saṅkāśam sunāsat nāma viśrutam tasya eva dakṣiṇe kūṭe viṃśat yojana vistaram dviṣaṣṭi yojana āyāmam hema prākāra toraṇam hṛṣṭa puṣṭa avaliptānām āvāsāḥ kāmarūpiṇām autkacānām pramuditam rākṣasānām mahā puram madhyame tu mahā kūṭe devakūṭasya vai gireḥ suvarṇa maṇi pāṣāṇaiḥ citraiḥ ślakṣaṇataraiḥ śubhaiḥ śākhā śata sahasra ādyaiḥ na eka āroha samākulam ramyam hi avirala chāyam daśa yojana maṇḍalam tatra bhūtavaṭat nāma nānā bhūta gaṇa ālayam varāha gaja siṃha ṛkṣa śārdūla karabha ānanaiḥ gṛdhra ulūka mukhaiḥ ca eva meṣa uṣṭra aja mahā mukhaiḥ nānā varṇa ākṛti dharaiḥ nānā saṃsthāna saṃsthitaiḥ a śūnyam abhavat nityam mahā pāriṣadaiḥ tathā tatra bhūtapateḥ bhūtāḥ nityampūjām prayuñjate jharjharaiḥ śaṅkha paṭahaiḥ bherī ḍiṇḍima gomukhaiḥ visphūrjita śataiḥ tatra pūjā yuktāḥ gaṇeśvarāḥ prītāḥ purāri pramathāḥ tatra krīḍā parāḥ sadā sthāne tasmin mahādevaḥ sākṣāt loka śivaḥ śivaḥ iti śrī mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte bhuvanavinyāsaḥ nāma catvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca kailāsam deva bhaktānām ālayam sukṛta ātmanām yojanānām śata āyāme pañcāśat ca tathāyatam suvarṇa maṇi citrābhiḥ anekābhiḥ alaṃkṛtam mahā bhavana mālābhiḥ bhūṣitam na eka vistaram nagarantat anādhṛṣyam ṛddhi yuktam mudā yutam tasya madhye sabhā ramyā nānā kanaka maṇḍitā vipulā nāma vikhyātā vipula stambha toraṇā tatra tat puṣpakam nāma nānā ratna vibhūṣitam mahā vimānam ruciram sarva kāma guṇaiḥ yutam manojavam kāma gamam hema jāla vibhūṣitam vāhanam yakṣarājasya kuberasya mahātmanaḥ aṣṭau ete akṣayāḥ divyāḥ dhaneśasya mahātmanaḥ mahā nidhānāḥ tiṣṭhanti sabhāyām ratna sañcitāḥ tathā indra agni yama ādīnām devānām apsaraḥ gaṇaiḥ teṣām kailāsaḥ āvāsaḥ yatra yakṣeśvaraḥ prabhuḥ kṛtvā pūrvam upasthānam yakṣa indrasya mahātmanaḥ paścāt gacchanti ye yasya vihitāḥ paricārakāḥ suvarṇa maṇi sopānā nānā puṣpa utkaṭa utkaṭā jāmbūnada mayaiḥ padmaiḥ gandha sparśa guṇa anvitaiḥ tathā kumuda khaṇḍaiḥ ca mahā padmaiḥ alaṅkṛtā upaspṛṣṭa jalā ramyā vāpī mandākinī tathā tathā alakanandā ca nandā ca saritām varā tasya eva śailarājasya pūrve kūṭe pariśrutāḥ sahasra yojana āyāmāḥ triṃśat yojana vistarāḥ daśa gandharvanagarāḥ samṛddhyā parayā yutāḥ mahā bhavana mālābhiḥ anekābhiḥ vibhūṣitāḥ subāhu harikeśa ādyāḥ citrasena jara ādayaḥ daśa gandharva rājānaḥ dīpta vahni parākramāḥ nānā dhātu śataiḥ citraiḥ siddha deva ṛṣi sevite aśīti yojana āyāmam catvāriṃśat pravistaram mahā yakṣa ālayāni atra triṃśat āḍhyāni me śrṛṇu mahāmāli sunetra ādyāḥ tathā maṇivara ādayaḥ udīrṇāḥ yakṣa rājānaḥ tatra triṃśat sadā babhuḥ yeṣām adhipatiḥ devaḥ śrīmān vaiśravaṇaḥ prabhuḥ arṇavāt arṇavam yāvat pūrvapaścāyate acale kinnarāṇām pura śatam niviṣṭam vai vkacid vkacid na eka śrṛṅga kalāpasya śailarājasya kukṣiṣu nara nārī pramuditam hṛṣṭa puṣṭa jana ākulam yatra rāja śatam teṣām dīptānām bala śālinām kirāta rūpiṇā ca eva yatra rudreṇa krīḍitam yatra ca eva kṛtam tābhyām jambūdvīpa avalokanam yatra tāḥ sammudā yuktāḥ nānā bhūta gaṇaiḥ yutāḥ citra puṣpa phala upetāḥ rudrasya ākrīḍa bhūmayaḥ hṛṣṭāḥ giri darī vāsāḥ kṛśa udaryyaḥ eva abyantare kūṭe nānā dhātu vibhūṣite taṭe niṣadha kūṭasya ślakṣṇa cāru śilā tale rukma kāñcana niryūham tapta kāñcana toraṇam aneka valabhī kūṭa pralolī śata saṅkaṭam harmya prāsādam atulam tapta ālaye guhāpraveśam nagaram śailakukṣau durāsadam tathā eva paścime kūṭe pārijāta śiloccaye deva dānava bhāgānām samṛddhāni purāṇi tu upāsate atra śrīmantam tārā patim aninditam ṛṣi kinnara gandharvāḥ sākṣāt devam tamonudam upāsate mahātmānam yakṣa gandharva dānavāḥ ṛṣi siddha anucarite nānā bhūta gaṇa ālaye trayāṇām deva mukhyānām trīṇi eva āyatanāni ca nārāyaṇasya āyatanam pūrva kūṭe dvijottamāḥ madhyame brahmaṇaḥ sthānam śaṅkarasya tu paścime ijānāḥ abhipūjyante devadevāḥ mahā balāḥ tathā purāṇi ramyāṇi deśe ca eva yakṣa gandharva nāgānām triśrṛṅge varaparvate yakṣāṇām kinnarāṇām ca gandharvāṇām sahasraśas nāgānām rākṣasānām ca daityānām ca mahā bale vihaṅga saṅgha saṃghuṣṭam nānā satva niṣevitam haṃsa kāraṇḍava ākīrṇam matta ṣaṭpada sevitam nānā satva gaṇa ākīrṇam vihaṅgaiḥ upaśobhitam cārutīrtha susambādham triṃśat yojana maṇḍalam tatra ānandajalat nāma mahā puṇya jalam saraḥ tatra nāga patiḥ ścaṇḍaḥ ścaṇḍaḥ nāma durāsadaḥ śata śīrṣā mahābhāgaḥ viṣṇu cakra aṅka cihnitaḥ iti evam aṣṭau vijñeyāḥ vicitrāḥ devaparvatāḥ puraiḥ āyatanaiḥ puṇyaiḥ puṇya udaiḥ ca sarovaraiḥ nānā ratna prabhāsaiḥ ca na ekaiḥ ca maṇi parvataiḥ śuddhaiḥ manaḥ śilā jālaiḥ bhāsvaraiḥ aruṇa bhūṣaṇaiḥ catvāraḥ na eka varṇa ādyāḥ mahā dvīpāḥ pariśrutāḥ bhadrāḥ ca bharatāḥ ca eva ketumālāḥ ca paścimāḥ uttarāḥ kuravaḥ ca eva kṛta puṇya pratiśrayāḥ sā eṣā catur mahā dvīpā nānā dvīpa samākulā vāyuprokte bhuvanavinyāsaḥ nāma ekacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca mahā ogha toyāḥ nadyaḥ ca tāḥ śrṛṇudhvam yathākramam ādhāraḥ sarva bhūtānām devānām amṛta ākaraḥ tasmāt pravṛttā puṇya udā nadī hi ākāśa gāminī sā jyotiṣi nivartantī jyotiḥ gaṇa niṣevitā tārāka oji sahasrāṇām nabhasaḥ ca samāyatāḥ māhendreṇa gaja indreṇa ākāśa patha yāyinā krīḍitā hi antara tale yā sā vikṣobhita udakā siddhaiḥ upaspṛṣṭa jalā mahā puṇya jalā śivā vāyunā preryamāṇā ca aneka ābhoga gāminī catvāri aśītiḥ pratatāḥ yojanānām samantataḥ vegena kurvatī merum sā prayātā pradakṣiṇam meru kūṭa taṭa antebhyaḥ utkṛṣṭebhyaḥ nivartitāḥ vikīryamāṇa salilā caturddhā a saṃsṛta udakā ṣaṣṭi yojana sāhasram nirālambanam ambaram sā caturṣu abhitas ca eva mahā pādeṣu śobhanā puṇyā mandara pūrveṇa patitā hi mahā nadī pūrveṇa aṃśena devānām sarva siddha gaṇa ālayam tathā caitraratham ramyam plāvayantī pradakṣiṇam aruṇodāt nivṛttā atha śīta ante ramya nirjhare śaile siddha gaṇa āvāse nipapāta su gāminī sītā nāma mahā puṇyā nadīnām pravarā nadī sā nikuñja niruddhā tu aneka ābhoga gāminī śītāntā śikharāt bhraṣṭā su kuñje vara parvate nipapāta mahābhāgā tasmāt api sumañjasam tasmāt mālyavatam śailam bhāvayantī kukṣi samudra antā krameṇa pṛthivīm gatā sā evam sthalī sahasrāṇi śailarāja śatāni ca vanāni ca vicitrāṇi sarāṃsi vividhāni ca srāvayantī mahābhāgā visphāreṣu avalīka dā nadī sahasra anugatā pravṛttā dvijaśārdūla ghorāṇām api pāpmanām śaṅkarasya aṅka saṃsparśāt mahādevasya dhīmataḥ atho anyena abhidhānena khyātāḥ nadyaḥ sahasraśas tasmāt himavataḥ gaṅgā gatā sā tu mahā nadī evam gaṅgā iti nāmnā kṛdbhiḥ niṣevitam api yā tryambakasya eṣā tridaśaiḥ sevita udakā vāyu vegā gata ābhogā latā iva bhrāmitā punar meru kūṭa taṭāt bhraṣṭā prahataiḥ svādita udakā vistīryyamāṇa salilā nirmmala aṃśuka sannibhā tasya kūṭe ambara nadī siddha cāraṇa sevitā pradakṣiṇam atha āvṛtya patitā sā tu gāminī deva bhrājam mahā bhrājam sa vaibhrājam mahā vanam plāvayantī mahābhāgā nānā puṣpa phala udakā pradakṣiṇam prakurvāṇāḥ nānā vana vibhūṣitāḥ praviṣṭā sita udam vimala udakam sā sita udāt viniṣkrāntā supakṣam parvvatam gatā supakṣakūṭa taṭa gā tasmāt ca saṃśita udakā nipapāta mahābhāgā ramaṇyam śikhi parvvatam śikheḥ ca parvatāt kaṅkam kaṅkāt vaiḍhūryya parvvatam vaiḍhūryyāt kapilam śailam tasmāt ca gandhamādanam piñjarāt sarasam yātā tasmāt ca kumudācalam mukuṭāt śaila śikharāt kṛṣṇam yātāḥ pradakṣiṇam sarovaram mahā puṇyam mahābhāga niṣevitam tatra āviveśa kalyāṇī mahā bhadram sitodakā bhadrasoma iti nāmnā hi mahā pārāḥ mahā javāḥ mahānadī mahā puṇyā mahābhadrā vinirgatā nā eka nirjhara vapra āḍhyā śaṃkhakūṭa taṭe tu sā tatra kūṭe giri taṭe nipapāta āśu gāminī śaṃkha kūṭa taṭāt bhraṣṭā papāta vṛṣaparvvatam vṛṣaparvvatāt vatsa girim nāgaśailam tatas gatāḥ tasmāt nīlam naga śreṣṭham saṃprāptāḥ varṣaparvvatam nīlāt kapiñjalam ca eva indranīlam ca nimnagā tatas param mahānīlam hemaśrṛṅgam ca sā yayau hemaśrṛṅgāt gatā śvetam śvetāt ca sunagam yayau sunagāt śataśrṛṅgam ca saṃprāptā sā mahā nadī śataśrṛṅgāt mahā śailam puṣkaram puṣpa maṇḍitam puṣkarāt ca mahā śailam dvirājam su mahā balam varāhaparvvatam tasmāt mayūram ca śiloccayam mayūrāt ca eka śikharam kandara udara maṇḍitam pavanena īrita udakā plāvayantī mahābhāgā prayātā paścima arṇavam kandara udara vibhraṣṭā tasmāt api taraṅgiṇī na eka bhogā papāta urvīm citra puṣpa uḍhupa utkacā plāvayantī pramuditā uttarān sā kurūn śivā mahā dvīpasya madhyena prayātā sa uttarārṇavam evam tāḥ tu mahā nadyaḥ catasraḥ vimala udakāḥ mahā giri taṭa bhraṣṭāḥ saṃprayātāḥ caturdiśam tat sā iyam kathita prāyā pṛthivī bahu vistarā meru śaila mahā ākīrṇā aviśat ca sarvatodiśam catur mahā dvīpavatī catur ākrīḍa kānanā catuṣketu mahāvṛkṣā caturvara sarasvatī catur mahā śailavatī catur bhujaga saṃśrayā aṣṭa uttara mahā śailā tathā aṣṭa vara parvatā iti śrī mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte bhuvanavinyāsaḥ nāma dvicatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca gandhamādana pārśve tu sphītā ca upari gaṇḍikā dvātriṃśatam sahasrāṇi yojanaiḥ pūrva paścimā asya āyāma śaca vatustriṃśat sahasrāṇi pramāṇataḥ tatra te śubha karmāṇaḥ ketumālāḥ pariśrutāḥ tatra kālāḥ narāḥ sarve mahāsattvāḥ mahā balāḥ striyaḥ ca utpala patra ābhāḥ sarvāḥ tāḥ priya darśanāḥ tatra divyaḥ mahā vṛkṣaḥ panasaḥ ṣaṣ rasa āśrayaḥ īśvaraḥ brahmaṇaḥ putraḥ kāma cārī manojavaḥ pārśve mālyavataḥ ca api pūrve tu gaṇḍikā āyāmataḥ atha vistārāt yathā eva apara gaṇḍikā bhadrāśvāḥ tatra vijñeyāḥ nityam mudita mānasāḥ bhadram sāla vanam tatra kāla āmrāḥ ca mahā drumāḥ tatra te puruṣāḥ śvetāḥ mahāsattvāḥ mahā balāḥ striyaḥ kumuda varṇa ābhāḥ sundaryyaḥ priya darśanāḥ candra prabhā aśvandra varṇāḥ pūrṇa candra nibha ānanāḥ candra śītala gātrāḥ ca striyaḥ ca utpala gandhikāḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi teṣām āyuḥ nirāmayam kāla āmrasya rasam pītvā sarvadā sithara yauvanāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ pramāṇam varṇam āyuḥ ca yāthātathyena kīrtitam caturṇām api dvīpānām samāsāt na tu vistarāt uvāca bhadrāśvānām yathā cihnam kīrtitam kīrti varddhanāḥ tat śṛṇudhvam tu kārtsnyena pūrva siddhaiḥ udāhṛtam pūrveṇa dikṣu sarvāsu yathāvat ca prakīrtitam kula acalānām pañcānām nadīnām ca viśeṣataḥ tathā janapadānām ca yathā dṛṣṭam yathāśrutam śaivālaḥ varṇamālā agraḥ korañjaḥ ca acala uttamaḥ śveta varṇaḥ ca nīlaḥ ca pañca ete kulaparvatāḥ teṣām prasūtiḥ anye api parvatāḥ bahu vistarāḥ koṭi koṭiḥ kṣitau jñeyāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas taiḥ vimiśrāḥ janapadaiḥ nānā sattva samākulāḥ nānā prakāra jātīyāḥ tu aneka nṛpa pālitāḥ nāmadheyaiḥ ca nikrāntaiḥ śrīmadbhiḥ puruṣa ṛṣabhaiḥ adhyāsitāḥ janapadāḥ kīrtanīyāḥ ca śobhitāḥ teṣām tu nāmadheyāni rāṣṭrāṇi vividhāni ca giri antara niviṣṭāni sameṣu viṣameṣu ca tathā su maṅgalāḥ śuddhāḥ candra kāntāḥ su nandanāḥ vrajakāḥ nīlaśaileyāḥ sauvīrāḥ vijayasthalāḥ mahā sthalāḥ su kāmāḥ ca mahā keśāḥ su mūrddhajāḥ vāta raṃhāḥ sa upasaṅgāḥ parivāyāḥ parācakāḥ sambha vakrāḥ mahā netrāḥ śaivāla astanapāḥ tathā kumudāḥ śākamuṇḍāḥ ca uraḥ saṅkīrṇa bhaumakāḥ sa udakāḥ vatsakāḥ ca eke vārāhāḥ hāra vāmakāḥ śaṅkha ākhyāḥ bhāvisandrāḥ ca uttarāḥ haimabhaumakāḥ kṛṣṇabhaumāḥ subhaumāḥ ca mahābhaumāḥ ca kīrtitāḥ ete ca anye ca vikhyātāḥ nānā janapadāḥ mayā te pibanti mahāpuṇyām mahāgaṅgām mahā nadīm ādau trailokya vikhyātā śītā śīta ambu vāhinī cakrā vakrā ca kañcī ca surasā ca apagā uttamā śākhāvatī ca indranadī meghā maṅgāravāhinī kāverī haritoyā ca somāvarttā śatahradā vanamālā vasumatī pampā pampāvatī śubhā suvarṇā pañca varṇā ca tathā puṇyā vapuṣmatī maṇi vaprā su vaprā ca brahma bhāgā śilā āśinī kṛṣṇatoyā ca puṇyodā tathā nāgapadī śubhā śaivālinī maṇitaṭā kṣārodā ca aruṇāvatī tathā viṣṇupadī ca eva mahā puṇyā mahānadī hiraṇyavāhinīlā ca skandamālā surāvatī vāmodā ca patākā ca vetālī ca mahā nadī etāḥ gaṅgāḥ mahā nadyaḥ nāyikāḥ parikīrtitāḥ kṣudra nadyaḥ tu asaṃkhyātāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas pūrva dvīpasya vohinyaḥ puṇyavatyaḥ ca kīrtitāḥ kīrttanena api ca etāsām pūtaḥ syāt iti me matiḥ samṛddha rāṣṭram sphītam ca nānā janapada ākulam nānā vṛkṣa vana uddeśam nānā naga su veṣṭitam nara nārī gaṇa ākīrṇam nityam pramuditam śivam bahu dhānya dhana upetam nānā nṛpati pālitam upetam kīrtana śataiḥ nānā ratna ākarākaram tasmin deśe samākhyātāḥ hema śaṅkha dala prabhāḥ mahā kāyāḥ mahā vīryāḥ puruṣāḥ puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ sambhāṣaṇam darśanam ca sama sthāna upasevanam devaiḥ saha mahābhāgāḥ kurvate tatra vai prajāḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi teṣām āyuḥ prakīrtitam dharma adharma viśeṣaḥ ca na teṣu asti mahātmasu te bhaktyā śaṅkaram devam gaurīm parama vaiṣṇavīm ijyā pūjā namaskārān tābhyām nityam prayuñjate iti śrī mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte bhuvanavinyāsaḥ nāma tricatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca nisargaḥ eṣa vikhyātaḥ bhadrāśvānām yathārtha vat śrṛṇudhvam ketumālānām vistareṇa prakīrttanam kula acalānām saptānām nadīnām ca viśeṣataḥ tathā janapadānām ca vistaram śrotum arhatha viśālaḥ kambalaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ jayantaḥ hariparvataḥ teṣām prasūtiḥ anye api parvatāḥ bahu vistarāḥ koṭi koṭi śatāḥ jñeyāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas taiḥ vimiśrāḥ janapadāḥ nānā jāti samākulāḥ nānā prakāra vijñeyāḥ tu aneka nṛpa pālitāḥ te nāmadheyaiḥ vikrāntāḥ vividhāḥ prathitāḥ bhuvi adhyāsitāḥ janapadaiḥ kīrttanaiḥ ca vibhūṣitāḥ teṣām sanāmadheyāni rāṣṭrāṇi vividhāni ca giri antara niviṣṭāni sameṣu viṣameṣu ca yathā eha kathitāḥ paurāḥ go manuṣya kapotakāḥ tad sukhāḥ bhramarāḥ yūthāḥ māheya acalakūṭakāḥ kūṭakambalamauṣīyāḥ samudrāntarakāḥ tathā karambhavāḥ kucāḥ śvetāḥ suvarṇa kaṭakāḥ śubhāḥ śveta aṅgāḥ kṛṣṇa pādāḥ ca vihagā kapila karṇikāḥ ati ākarāla go jvālāḥ hīna anāvana pātakāḥ mahiṣāḥ kumuda ābhāḥ ca karavāṭāḥ saha utkacāḥ śu nakā kanāsāḥ mahānāsāḥ vanāsa gajabhūmikāḥ karañja mañjamāḥ vāhāḥ kiṣkiṇḍī pāṇḍu bhūmikīḥ kuberāḥ dhūmajāḥ jaṅgāḥ vaṅgāḥ rājīva kokilāḥ vācāṅgāḥ ca mahāṅgāḥ ca madhaureyāḥ su recakāḥ pittalāḥ kācalāḥ ca eva śravaṇāḥ mattakāsikāḥ godāvāḥ bakulāḥ vāṅgāḥ vaṅgakāḥ modakāḥ kalāḥ te pibanti mahābhāgāḥ prathamān tu mahā nadīm su vaprām puṇya salilām mahā nāga niṣevitām kambalām tāmasīm śyāmām sumedhām bakulām nadīm vikīrṇām śikhi mālām ca tathā darbhāvatīm api bhadrānadīm śukanadīm palāśān ca mahā nadīm bhīmām prabhañjanām kāñcīm puṇyām ca eva kuśāvatīm dakṣām śākavatīm ca eva mahā nadīm candrāvatīm sumūlām ca ṛṣabhān ca āpagā uttamām nadīm samudramālām ca tathā campāvatīm api eka akṣām puṣkalām vāhām suvarṇām nandi kālindīm ca eva puṇya udām bhāratīm ca mahā nadīm sītodāmpātikām brāhmīm viśālām ca mahā nadīm pīvarīm kumbhakārīm ca ruṣā ñca eva āpagā uttamām mahiṣīm mānuṣīm daṇḍām tathā nadanadīm śubhām etān ca anyān ca pīyante bahvayaḥ hi saritā uttamāḥ deva ṛṣi siddha caritāḥ puṇya udāḥ pāpa hāḥ śubhāḥ nānā janapada āsphītam mahā āpagā vibhūṣitam nānā ratna ogha sampūrṇam nityam pramuditam śivam udīrṇam dhana dhānya arthaiḥ nara vāsaiḥ samantataḥ sanniviṣṭam mahā dvīpam paścimam sukṛta ātmanām nisargaḥ ketumālānām eṣa vaḥ parikīrttitaḥ iti śrī mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte bhuvanavinyāsaḥ nāma catuśvatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca uttarāṇām ca varṣāṇām dakṣiṇānām ca sarvaśas ācakṣva naḥ yathātathyam ye ca parvata vāsinaḥ uvāca varṣam ramaṇakam nāma jāyante tatra mānavāḥ sarva ṛtu kāma dāḥ sattvāḥ jarā durgandha varjitāḥ śukra abhijana sampannāḥ sarve ca priya darśanāḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi śatāni daśa pañca ca jīvanti te mahābhāgā sadā hṛṣṭāḥ nara uttamāḥ uttareṇa tu śvetasya śrṛṅgasāhvasya dakṣiṇe varṣam hiraṇyatam nāma yatra hairaṇyatī nadī mahā balāḥ su tejaskāḥ jāyante tatra mānavāḥ sarva ṛtu kāma dāḥ satvāḥ dhaninaḥ priya darśanāḥ ekādaśa sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām te amita ojasaḥ āyuṣpramāṇam jīvanti śatāni daśa pañca ca tasmin varṣe mahā vṛkṣaḥ lakucaḥ ṣaṣ rasa āśrayaḥ tasya pītvā phala rasam tatra jīvanti mānavāḥ trīṇi śrṛṅgavataḥ śrṛṅgāṇi ucchritāni mahānti ca ekam maṇi mayam teṣām ekam ca eva hiraṇyayam tatra vṛkṣāḥ madhu phalāḥ nityam puṣpa phala upagāḥ vastrāṇi ca prasūyante phaleṣu ābharaṇāni ca sarva kāma phalāḥ tatra vkacid vṛkṣāḥ manoramāḥ apare kṣīriṇaḥ nāma vṛkṣāḥ tatra manoramāḥ ye kṣaranti sadā kṣīram ṣaṣ rasam hi amṛta upamam sarvā maṇi mayī bhūmiḥ sūkṣma kāñcana vālukā sarva atas sukha saṃsparśā niṣpaṅkā nīrujā śubhā deva lokāt cyutāḥ tatra jāyante mānavāḥ śubhāḥ mithunāni prasūyante striyaḥ ca ati manoharāḥ te ca tam kṣīriṇam vṛkṣam pibanti hi amṛta upamam samam śīlam ca rūpam ca mriyante ca eva te samam anāmayāḥ hi aśokāḥ ca nityam sukha niṣeviṇaḥ trayodaśa sahasrāṇi śatāni daśa pañca ca jīvanti te mahā vīryāḥ na ca anya strī niṣeviṇaḥ kurūṇām api ca eteṣām śrṛṇudhvam vistareṇa tu jārudheḥ śailarājasya api uttareṇa uttarasya hi tābhyām kūṭa śataiḥ na ekaiḥ tat dvīpam upasevitam candrakāntaḥ ca śailaḥ ca sūryakāntaḥ ca sānumān yayoḥ madhye na sā yātā bhadrasomā mahā nadī sahasraśas ca nadyaḥ anyāḥ prasanna surasa udakāḥ paryāpta udāḥ kurūṇām hi snāna pāna avagāhanaiḥ tathā anyāḥ kṣīra vāhinyaḥ mahā nadyaḥ sahasraśas dadhnaḥ śatahradāḥ ca anyāḥ tatas svādu anna parvataḥ gandha varṇa rasa āḍhyāni mūlāni ca phalāni ca pañca yojana mānāni mahā gandhāni sarvaśas nānā varṇa prakārāṇi puṣpāṇi ca sahasraśas gandha varṇa rasa āḍhyāni sparśa upetāni sarvaśas tamāla aguru gandhānām candanānām vanāni ca vṛkṣa gulma latā ḍhayāni vanāni su sukhāni ca ṣaṭpadaiḥ upagītāni dvijaiḥ ca anyaiḥ dvijottamāḥ pajha utpala vana āḍhyāni sarāṃsi ca sahasraśas bhakṣya mālya samṛddhāḥ ca bahu mālya anulepanāḥ manohara mukhaiḥ citraiḥ pakṣi saṅghaiḥ nikūjitāḥ śayana āsana upabhogāḥ ca aneka guṇa vistarāḥ vihāra bhūmayaḥ ramyāḥ sarva ṛtuṣu sukha pradāḥ ākrīḍāḥ sarvatas sphītāḥ maṇi hema pariṣkṛtāḥ śilāgṛhāḥ vṛkṣagṛhāḥ vareṇyāḥ kadalī gṛhāḥ latāgṛha sahasrāṇi su sukhāni samantataḥ śuddha śaṅkha dala ābhāni bhūmi veśma śatāni ca tapanīya gavākṣāṇi māṇijāla antarāṇi ca mahā vṛkṣa sahasrāṇi vareṇyāni ca sarvaśas nānā ākārāṇi vāsāṃsi sūkṣmāṇi su sukhāni ca mṛdaṅga veṇu paṇava vīṇā ādyāḥ bahu vistarāḥ phalanti kalpavṛkṣāṇām sahasrāṇi śatāni ca pravāti ca anilaḥ tatra nānā puṣpa adhivāsitaḥ tatra svarga paribhraṣṭāḥ jāyante hi narāḥ sadā candra kāntāḥ nara varāḥ śyāma aṅkāḥ pūrva kūla jāḥ śyāma avadātāḥ sukhinaḥ sūrya kāntāḥ varāḥ prajāḥ tasmin deśe narāḥ śreṣṭāḥ deva sattva parākramāḥ sadā vihāriṇaḥ sarve kāma vṛttyā su varcasaḥ valaya aṅgada keyūra hāra kuṇḍala bhūṣitāḥ sragviṇaḥ citra mukuṭāḥ citra ācchādana vāsasaḥ ajīrṇa yauvana dharāḥ su priyāḥ priya darśanāḥ prajāḥ varṣa sahasrāṇi jīvanti su bahūni uta na tāḥ prasava dharmiṇyaḥ na vaṃśa prakṣayaḥ vidhiḥ mithunam jāyate vṛkṣāt upakṣamam anīdṛśam sāmānya vibhavāḥ sarve mamatva parivarjitāḥ uttarāṇām kurūṇām tu dakṣiṇe samudram ūrmi mālā āḍhyam nānā svara vibhūṣitam nānā puṣpa phala upetam samṛddhyā parayā yutam candra tulya prabhaiḥ kāntaiḥ candra ākāraiḥ su lakṣaṇaiḥ mahā sānu darī kuñjaiḥ vividhaiḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ tasmāt śailāt mahā puṇyā candra aṃśu vimala udakā pravahati uttama nadī candra āvarttā taraṅgiṇī tatra candramasaḥ nāmnā śailaḥ sa tu pariśrutaḥ candradvīpam mahā dvīpam prakāśam divi ca iha ca tatra candra pratīkāśāḥ pūrṇa candra nibha ānanāḥ candra kāntāḥ prajāḥ sarvāḥ vimalāḥ candra daivatāḥ atyanta dhārmikāḥ saumyāḥ satya sandhāḥ su tejasaḥ prajāḥ tatra sat ācārāḥ daśa varṣa śata āyuṣaḥ daśa yojana sāhasram samantāt parimaṇḍalam dvīpam bhadrākaram nāma nānā puṣpa upaśobhitam prabhūta dhana dhānya āḍhyam aneka nṛpa pālitam nityam pramuditam sphītam mahā śailaiḥ ca śobhitam tatra bhadrāsanam vāyoḥ nānā ratnaiḥ ca maṇḍitam tapanīya suvarṇa ābhāḥ tapanīya vibhūṣitāḥ vīryavantaḥ mahābhāgāḥ pañca varṣa śata āyuṣaḥ satya sandhāḥ mudā yuktāḥ prajāḥ tāḥ vāyu daivatāḥ uvāca evam eva nisargaḥ ayam varṣāṇām bhārate yuge dṛṣṭaḥ parama tattva jñaiḥ bhūyas kim kīrttayāmi te ākhyāte tu evam ṛṣayaḥ sūta putreṇa dhīmatā ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ yat idam bhāratam varṣa yasmin svāyambhuva ādayaḥ etat śrutvā vacaḥ teṣām abravīt lomaharṣaṇaḥ paurāṇikaḥ tadā sūtaḥ ṛṣīṇām bhāvitātmanām uvāca nisargaḥ eṣa vikhyātaḥ kurūṇām tu yathārthavat pūrva paśca āyatasya asya dakṣiṇena dvijottamāḥ tathā janapadānām ca vistaram śrotum arhatha atra vaḥ varṇayiṣyāmi varṣe asmin bhārate prajāḥ varṣam yat bhāratam nāma yatra iyam bhāratī prajā bharaṇāt ca prajānām vai manuḥ bharataḥ ucyate tatas svargaḥ ca mokṣaḥ ca madhyaśrāntaḥ ca gamyate bhāratasya asya varṣasya nava bhedāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ayantu navamaḥ teṣām dvīpaḥ sāgara saṃvṛtaḥ yojanāṃnām sahasram tu dvīpaḥ ayam dakṣiṇa uttaram āyataḥ hi ā kumārikyāt āṅga a prabhavāt ca vai dvīpaḥ hi upaniviṣṭaḥ ayam mlecchaiḥ anteṣu nityaśas pūrve kirātāḥ hi asya ante paścime yavanāḥ smṛtāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ madhye śūdrāḥ ca bhāgaśas teṣām saṃvyavahāraḥ ayam varttate tu parasparam dharma artha kāma saṃyuktaḥ varṇānām tu sva karmasu saṅkalpa pañcamānām tu āśramāṇām yathāvidhi iha svarga apavarga artham pravṛttiḥ yeṣu mānuṣī ayam lokaḥ tu vai samrāj antarikṣaḥ virāj smṛtaḥ svarāj anyaḥ smṛtaḥ lokaḥ punar vakṣyāmi vistaram sapta ca asmin su parvāṇaḥ viśrutāḥ kulaparvatāḥ mahendraḥ malayaḥ sahyaḥ śuktimān ṛkṣa parvataḥ teṣām sahasraśas ca anye parvatāḥ tu samīpa gāḥ abhijātāḥ sarva guṇāḥ vipulāḥ citra sānavaḥ pātandhamaḥ nāma giriḥ tathā pāṇḍura parvataḥ śrīparvataḥ ca kāruḥ ca kūṭaśailaḥ giriḥ tathā anye tebhyaḥ parijñātāḥ hrasvāḥ su alpa upajīvinaḥ taiḥ vimiśrāḥ jatapadāḥ ārya mlecchāḥ ca nityaśas pīyante yaiḥ imāḥ nadyaḥ gaṅgā sindhuḥ sarasvatī śatadruḥ candrabhāgā ca yamunā sarayūḥ tathā irāvatī vitastā ca vipāśā devikā kuhūḥ gomatī dhutapāpā ca bāhudā ca dṛṣadvatī kauśikī ca tṛtīyā tu niścīrā gaṇḍakī tathā iti etāḥ himavat pāda niḥsṛtāḥ varṇāśā candanā ca eva satīrā mahatī tathā śiprā hi avantī ca tathā pāriyātra āśrayāḥ smṛtāḥ śoṇaḥ mahānadaḥ ca eva narmadā su mahā drumāḥ mandākinī daśārṇā ca citrakūṭā tathā eva ca tamasā pippalā śroṇī karatoyā piśācikā nīlotpalā vipāśā ca jambulā vāluvāhinī ṛkṣa pādāt prasūtāḥ tāḥ nadyaḥ maṇi nibha udakāḥ tāpī payoṣṇī nirvindhyā madrā ca niṣadhā nadī venvā vaitaraṇī ca eva śitibāhuḥ kumudvatī toyā ca eva mahāgaurī durgā ca antaśilā tathā vindhya pāda prasūtāḥ ca nadyaḥ puṇya jalāḥ śubhāḥ godāvarī bhīmarathī kṛṣṇā vaiṇī atha vañjulā tuṅgabhadrā suprayogā kāverī ca tathā āpagā dakṣiṇāpatha nadyaḥ tu sahya pādāt viniḥsṛtāḥ malaya abhijātāḥ tāḥ nadyaḥ sarvāḥ śīta jalāḥ śubhāḥ trisāmā ṛtukulyā ca ikṣulā tridivā ca yā lāṅgulinī vaṃśa dharāḥ mahendra tanayāḥ smṛtāḥ ṛṣīkā sukumārī ca mandagā mandavāhinī kūpā palāśinī ca eva śuktimat prabhavāḥ smṛtāḥ sarvāḥ puṇyāḥ sarasvatyaḥ sarvāḥ gaṅgāḥ samudra gāḥ viśvasya mātaraḥ sarvāḥ jagat pāpa harāḥ smṛtāḥ tāsām nadī upanadyaḥ api śataśas atha sahasraśas tāḥ tu ime kuru pāñcālāḥ śālvāḥ ca eva sa jāṅgalāḥ śūrasenāḥ bhadrakārāḥ bodhāḥ śatapatha īśvaraiḥ vatsāḥ kisaṣṇāḥ kulyāḥ ca kuntalāḥ kāśi kośalāḥ atha pārśve tilaṅgāḥ ca magadhāḥ ca vṛkaiḥ saha madhyadeśāḥ janapadāḥ prāyaśas amī prakīrtitāḥ pṛthivyām iha kṛtsnāyām sa pradeśaḥ manoramaḥ rāma priya artham svargaḥ ayam vṛkṣāḥ oṣadhayaḥ tathā bharadvājena muninā tad priya arthe avatāritāḥ vāhlīkāḥ vāḍhadhānāḥ ca ābhīrāḥ kālatoyakāḥ aparītāḥ ca śūdrāḥ ca pahnavāḥ carmakhaṇḍikāḥ gāndhārāḥ yavanāḥ ca eva sindhusauvīrabhadrakāḥ śakāḥ hradāḥ kulindāḥ ca paritāḥ hārapūrikāḥ ramaṭāḥ raddhakaṭakāḥ kekayāḥ daśamānikāḥ kṣatriya upaniveśāḥ ca vaiśya śūdra kulāni ca kāmbojāḥ daradāḥ ca eva barbarāḥ priya laukikāḥ pīnāḥ ca eva tuṣārāḥ ca pahlavāḥ bāhyatodarāḥ ātreyāḥ ca bharadvājāḥ prasthalāḥ ca kaserukāḥ lampākāḥ stanapāḥ ca eva pīḍikāḥ juhuḍaiḥ saha apagāḥ ca ali madrāḥ ca kirātānām ca jātayaḥ tomarāḥ haṃsamārgāḥ ca kāśmīrāḥ taṅgaṇāḥ tathā cūlikāḥ ca āhukāḥ ca eva pūrṇadarvāḥ tathā eva ca ete deśāḥ hi udīcyāḥ ca prācyān deśān nibodhata andhravākāḥ sujarakāḥ antargiri bahirgirāḥ tathā pravaṅga vaṅgeyāḥ māladāḥ mālavartinaḥ brahmottarāḥ pravijayāḥ bhārgavāḥ geyamarthakāḥ prāgjyotiṣāḥ ca muṇḍāḥ ca videhāḥ tāmaliptakāḥ mālāḥ magadha govindāḥ prācyām janapadāḥ smṛtāḥ atha apare janapadāḥ dakṣiṇāpatha vāsinaḥ pāṇḍyāḥ ca keralāḥ ca eva caulyāḥ kulyāḥ tathā eva ca setukāḥ mūṣikāḥ ca eva kumanāḥ vanavāsikāḥ mahārāṣṭrāḥ māhiṣakāḥ kaliṅgāḥ ca eva sarvaśas abhīrāḥ saha ca aiṣīkāḥ āṭavyāḥ ca varāḥ ca ye pulindrāḥ vindhyamūlīkāḥ vaidarbāḥ daṇḍakaiḥ saha nairmikāḥ kuntalāḥ āndhrāḥ udbhidāḥ nalakālikāḥ dākṣiṇātyāḥ ca vai deśāḥ aparān tān nibodhata śūrpākārāḥ kolavanāḥ durgāḥ kālītakaiḥ saha puleyāḥ ca surālāḥ ca rūpasāḥ tāpasaiḥ saha tathā tura sitāḥ ca eva sarve ca eva parakṣarāḥ nāsikya ādyoḥ ca ye ca anye ye ca eva antara narmadāḥ bhānukacchāḥ samāḥ heyāḥ sahasā śāśvataiḥ api kacchīyāḥ ca surāṣṭrāḥ ca anarttāḥ ca arbudaiḥ saha iti ete samparītāḥ ca śrṛṇudhvam vindhya vāsinaḥ mālavāḥ ca karūṣāḥ ca mekalāḥ ca utkalaiḥ saha uttamarṇāḥ daśārṇāḥ ca bhojāḥ kiṣkindhakaiḥ saha tosalāḥ kosalāḥ ca eva traipurāḥ vaidikāḥ tathā tumurāḥ tumburāḥ ca eva ṣaṣ surāḥ niṣadhaiḥ saha anupāḥ tuṇḍikerāḥ ca vītihotrāḥ hi avantayaḥ ete janapadāḥ sarve vindhya pṛṣṭha nivāsinaḥ atas deśān pravakṣyāmi parvata āśrayiṇaḥ ca ye nigarharāḥ haṃsamārgāḥ kṣupaṇāḥ taṅgaṇāḥ khasāḥ kuśa prāvaraṇāḥ ca eva hūṇāḥ darvāḥ sahūdakāḥ trigarttāḥ mālavāḥ ca eva kirātāḥ tāmasaiḥ saha kṛtam tretā dvāra pañca kaliḥ ca iti catuṣṭayam teṣām nisargam vakṣyāmi upariṣṭāt nibodhata iti śrī mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte bhuvanavinyāsaḥ nāma pañcacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca śuśrūṣavaḥ mudā yuktāḥ papracchuḥ lomaharṣaṇam ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ ācakṣva naḥ yathātattvam kīrttitam bhāratam tvayā yathā vipraiḥ yathā praśram viśeṣataḥ uvāca muni nirdiṣṭam purāṇam vihitam yathā uvāca śuśrūṣā yatra vaḥ viprāḥ tat śṛṇudhvam mudā yutāḥ pukṣakhaṇḍaḥ kimpuruṣe su mahān nandana upamaḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi sthitiḥ kimpuruṣe smṛtā suvarṇa varṇāḥ ca narāḥ striyaḥ ca apsarasā upamāḥ anāmayāḥ hi aśokāḥ ca sarve te śuddha mānasāḥ varṣe kimpuruṣe puṇye plakṣaḥ madhu vahaḥ śubhaḥ atas param kim puruṣāt harivarṣaḥ pracakṣyate mahārajata saṅkāśāḥ jāyante tatra mānavāḥ deva lokāt cyutāḥ sarve deva rūpāḥ ca sarvaśas harivarṣe narāḥ sarve pibanti ikṣu rasam śubham ekādaśa sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām tu mudā yutāḥ madhyamam yat mayā proktam nāmnā varṣam ilāvṛtam candra sūryau sa nakṣatrau aprakāśau ilāvṛte padma varṇāḥ padma prabhāḥ padma patra nibha īkṣaṇāḥ pakṣa patra sugandhāḥ ca jāyante tatra mānavāḥ jambū rasa phala āhārāḥ hi aniṣpandāḥ sugandhinaḥ deva lokāt cyutāḥ sarve jāyante hi ajara amarāḥ trayodaśa sahasrāṇi nara uttamāḥ āyuṣpramāṇam jīvanti te tu varṣe tu ilāvṛte yojanānām sahasrāṇi ṣaḍviṃśaḥ tasya vistaraḥ catur asraḥ samantāt ca śarāva ākāra saṃsthitaḥ udak dakṣiṇatas ca eva ā nīla niṣadha āyataḥ catvāriṃśat sahasrāṇi parivṛddhaḥ mahī talāt sahasram avagāḍhaḥ tu tāvat eva tu dhiṣṭitaḥ pūrveṇa mālyavān śailaḥ tad pramāṇaḥ prakīrtitaḥ teṣām madhye mahā meruḥ su pramāṇaḥ prakīrtitaḥ sarveṣām eva śailānām avagāḍhaḥ yathā bhavet vistaraḥ tad pramāṇaḥ syāt āyāme niyutaḥ smṛtaḥ vṛtta bhāvāt samudrasya mahī maṇḍala bhāvanaḥ āyāmāḥ parihīyante caturasrāḥ samastataḥ an āvṛttāḥ catuṣkeṇa bhidyante madhyama āgatāḥ prabhinna añjana saṅkāśā jambu rasavatī nadī meroḥ tu dakṣiṇe pārśve niṣadhasya uttareṇa tu sudarśanaḥ nāma mahā jambu vṛkṣaḥ sanātanaḥ tasya nāmnā samākhyātaḥ jambūdvīpe vanaspatiḥ yojanānām sahasram tu śata ca anya mahā drumaḥ utsedhaḥ vṛkṣarājaspa divam spṛśati sarvaśas aratnīnām śatāni aṣṭau ekaṣaṣṭi adhikāni tu phala pramāṇam saṃkhyātam ṛṣibhiḥ tattva darśibhiḥ merum pradakṣiṇīkṛtya vṛkṣam viśati adhas te pibanti sadā hṛṣṭāḥ jambu rasa phala āvṛtāḥ jambū rasa phalam pītvā na jarām prāpnuvanti te tatra jāmbūnadam nāma kanakam deva bhūṣaṇam jāyate tat sarveṣām varṣa vṛkṣāṇām śubhaḥ phala rasaḥ tu saḥ teṣām mūtram purīṣam ca dikṣu sarvāsu bhāgaśas īśvara anugrahāt bhūmiḥ mṛtān ca grasate tu tān rakṣaḥ piśācāḥ yakṣāḥ ca sarve haimavatāḥ smṛtāḥ hemakūṭe tu gandharvāḥ vijñeyāḥ sa apsaraḥ gaṇāḥ sarve nāgāḥ tu niṣadhe śeṣa vāsuki takṣakāḥ mahā merau trayastriṃśat bhramante yājñikāḥ surāḥ nīle tu vaiḍūrya maye siddha brahmarṣayaḥ matāḥ daityānām dānavānām ca śvetaparvataḥ ucyate śrṛṅgavān parvataḥ śreṣṭhaḥ pitṝṇām pratisañcaraḥ navasu eteṣu varṣeṣu yathā bhāga sthiteṣu vai bhūtāni upaniviṣṭāni gatimanti dhruvāṇi ca teṣām vivṛddhiḥ bahulā dṛśyate deva mānuṣoḥ na śakyā parisaṅkhyātum śraddheyā anu bubhūṣatā iti śrī mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte bhuvanavinyāsaḥ nāma ṣaṭcatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca savye himavataḥ pārśve kailāsaḥ nāma parvataḥ tasmin nivasati śrīmān kuberaḥ saha rākṣasaiḥ kailāsa pādāt sambhūtam puṇyam śīta jalam śubham tasmāt divyā prabhavati nadī mandākinī śubhā tasyāḥ tīre mahā divyam vanam caitraratham smṛtam yakṣa senāpatiḥ krūra guhyakaiḥ parivāritaḥ puṇyā mandākinī ca eva nimnagā acchodikā tathā kailāsāt dakṣiṇa prācyām śiva sattva oṣadhim gurum manaḥśilā mayam divyam piśaṅgam parvatam prati lohitaḥ hemaśrṛṅgaḥ tu giriḥ sūrya prabho mahān deva araṇyam viśokam ca tasya tīre mahā vanam kailāsāt dakṣiṇe pārśve krūra sattva auṣadham girim tasya pāde saraḥ puṇyam mānasam siddha sevitam tasmāt prabhavate puṇyā sarayūḥ loka bhāvanī tasyāḥ tīre vanam divyam vaibhrājam nāma viśrutam aruṇam parvata śreṣṭham rukma dhātu mayam prati śātakumbha mayaiḥ śubhraiḥ śilā jālaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ śata saṅkhyaiḥ tāpanīyaiḥ śrṛṅgaiḥ divam iva ullikhan muñjavān sa mahā divyaḥ durgaśailaḥ hima arcitaḥ tasya pādāt prabhavati śailodam nāma tat saraḥ tasmāt prabhavate hivyā śailodā nāma nimnagā sā cakṣuḥ śītayoḥ madhye praviṣṭā lavaṇa udadhim tasyāḥ tīre vanam divyam viśrutam surabhi iti vai hiraṇyaśrṛṅgaḥ su mahān divyaḥ maṇi mayaḥ giriḥ tasya pāde mahat divyam śubham kāñcana vālukam gaṅgā nimittam rājarṣiḥ uvāsa bahulāḥ samāḥ divam yāsyanti me pūrve gaṅgā toya pariplutāḥ yūpāḥ maṇi mayāḥ tatra citayaḥ ca hiraṇmayāḥ tatra iṣṭvā tu gataḥ śarvam śakraḥ sarvaiḥ suraiḥ saha dṛśyate bhāsvaraḥ rātrau devī tripathagā tu sā antarikṣam divam ca eva bhāvayantī bhuvaṃgatā bhava uttamāṅge patitā saṃruddhā yoga māyayā tasyāḥ ye bindavaḥ kecid kruddhāyāḥ patitāḥ kṣitau cintayāmāsa manasā śaṅkara kṣepaṇam prati bhittvā viśāmi pātālam srotasā gṛhya śaṅkaram jñātvā tasyāḥ abhiprāyam krūram devyā cikīrṣitam tirobhāvayitum buddhiḥ āsīt aṅgeṣu tām nadīm tasya avalepam tam buddhvā nadyāḥ kruddhaḥ tu śaṅkaraḥ etasmin eva kāle tu dṛṣṭvā rājānam agratas dhamanī santatam kṣīṇam kṣudhā parigata indriyam anena toṣitaḥ ca aham nadī artham pūrvam eva hi buddhvā asya vara dānam tu kopam niyatavān tu saḥ brahmaṇaḥ hi vacaḥ śrutvā pratijñā dhāraṇam tatas visarjayāmāsa saṃruddhām svena tejasā nadīm bhagīrathasya arthe tapasā ugreṇa toṣitaḥ tatas visṛjyamānāyāḥ srotaḥ tad saptata aṅgatam trayaḥ prācīm abhimukham pratīcīm trayaḥ eva tu nadyāḥ srotaḥ tu gaṅgāyāḥ pratyapadyata saptadhā nalinī hrādinī ca eva pāvanī ca eva prāk gatā sītā cakṣuḥ ca sindhuḥ ca pratīcīm diśam ākṣitāḥ saptamī tu anugā tāsām dakṣiṇena bhagīrathī tasmāt bhāgīrathī yā sā praviṣṭā lavaṇa udadhim saptā etāḥ bhāvayanti iha himāhvam varṣam eva tu prasūtāḥ sapta nadyaḥ tāḥ śubhāḥ bindusarā udbhavāḥ nānā deśān bhāvayantyaḥ mleccha prāyān ca sarvaśas upagacchanti tāḥ sarvāḥ yatas varṣati vāsanaḥ sirindhrān kuntalān cīnān barbharān yavasān druhān ruṣāṇān ca kuṇindān ca aṅaga loka varāḥ ca ye kṛtvā dvidhā sindhum arum sītā agāt paścima udadhim atha cīna marūn ca eva naṅgaṇān sarvamūlikān sādhrān tu sārān tampākān pahnavān daradān śakān etān janapadān cakṣuḥ srāvayantī gata udadhim daradān ca sa kāṃśmīrān gāndhārān varapān hradān śiva paurān indrahāsān vadātīn ca visarjayān śunāmukhān ca ūrddhva manūn siddha cāraṇa sovitān gandharvān kinnarān yakṣān rakṣaḥ vidyādhara uragān kalāpa grāmakān ca eva pāradān sīgaṇān khasān kirātān ca pulindān ca kurūn sa bharatān api pañcāla kāśi mātsyān ca magadha aṅgān tathā eva ca brahmottarān ca vaṅgān ca tāmaliptān tathā eva ca etān janapadān āryān gaṅgā bhāvayate śubhān tatas pratihatāḥ vindhye praviṣṭāḥ tatakṣva āhlādinī puṇyā prācīna abhimukhī yayau plāvayanti upabhogān ca niṣādānām ca jātayaḥ dhīvarān ṛṣikān ca eva tathā nīla mukhān api keralān uṣṭra karṇān ca kirātān api ca eva hi kāla udarān vivarṇān ca kumārān svarṇa bhūṣitān sā maṇḍale samudrasya tirobhūtā anupūrvataḥ tatas tu pāvanī ca eva prācīm eva diśam gatā tatā kha rathān ca eva indra śaṅku pathān api tatas ca nalinī ca āgāt prācīm āśām javena tu tomarān bhāvayanti iha haṃsa mārgān sahūhukān pūrvān deśān ca sevantī bhittvā sā bahudhā girīn karṇa prāvaraṇān ca eva prāpya ca aśva mukhān api nemi maṇḍala koṣṭe tu praviṣṭā sā mahā udadhim tāsām nadī upanadyaḥ ca śataśas atha sahasraśas upagacchanti tāḥ sarvāḥ yatas varṣati vāsavaḥ hariśrṛṅge tu vasati vidvān kaubairakaḥ vaśī yajña upetaḥ sa su mahān amita ojāḥ su vikramaḥ kubaira anucarāḥ hi ete catvāraḥ tad samāḥ smṛtāḥ evam eva tu vijñeyā ṛddhiḥ parvata vāsinām paraspareṇa dviguṇāḥ dharmataḥ kāmataḥ arthataḥ hemakūṭasya pṝṣṭe tu sāyanam nāma tat saraḥ tatra jāmbūnadī puṇyā yasyām jāmbūnadam śubham payaḥ dam tu saraḥ nīle su śubhram puṇḍarīka vat puṇḍarīkā payodā ca tasmāt nadyau vinirgate jyotsnā ca mṛgakāntā ca tasmāt dve saṃbabhūvatuḥ kalpavṛkṣa samākīrṇam madhu vat sarvatas sukham anye ca api atra vikhyātāḥ pajha mīna dvija ākulāḥ nāmnā rudrājayāḥ nāma dvādaśa udadhi sannibhāḥ tebhyaḥ śāntā ca mādhvī ca dve nadyau sambabhūvatuḥ ṛṣabhaḥ dundubhiḥ ca eva dhūmraḥ ca eva mahā giriḥ pūrva āyatāḥ mahabhāgāḥ nimnagāḥ lavaṇāmbhasi candrakaṅkaḥ tathā prāṇaḥ mahān agniḥ śiloccayaḥ udak yātāḥ udīcyāntāḥ avagāḍhāḥ mahā udadhim somakaḥ ca varāhaḥ ca nāradaḥ ca mahīdharaḥ pratīcīm āyatāḥ te vai praviṣṭāḥ lavaṇa udadhim āyatāḥ te mahā śailāḥ samudram dakṣiṇam prati candra mainākayoḥ madhyevidiśam dakṣiṇām prati nāmnā samudrapaḥ śrīmān aurvaḥ sa vaḍavāmukhaḥ dvādaśa ete praviṣṭāḥ hi parvatāḥ lavaṇa udadhim yat etat ṝśyate candre śvete kṛṣṇa śaśa ākṛtiḥ bhāratasya tu varṣasya bhedāḥ te nava kīrtitāḥ uttarottaram eteṣām varṣam uddiśyate guṇaiḥ ārogya āyuḥ pramāṇābhyām dharmataḥ kāmataḥ arthataḥ samanvitāni bhūtāni guṇaiḥ retaiḥ tu bhāgataḥ vasanti nānā jātīni teṣu varṣeṣu tāni vai iti eṣā adhārayat sarvam pṛtvī viśvam jagat sthitā iti mahāpurāṇe vāyu prokte bhuvanavinyāsaḥ nāma saptacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca daśa yojana sāhasram samatītya mahā arṇavam trīṇi eva tu sahasrāṇi yojanānām samāyatam atas tri bhāga vistīrṇam nānā puṣpa phala udayam yena kūṭa taṭaiḥ na ekaiḥ tat dvīpam samalaṃkṛtam vāpyaḥ tasya tu dvīpasya pravṛttāḥ vimala udakāḥ tasya śailasya chidreṣu vistīrṇeṣu āyateṣu ca anekeṣu samṛddhāni nānā ākārāṇi sarvvaśas nara nārī sama āḍhyāni muditāni mahānti ca teṣām tala praveśāni sahasrāṇi śatāni ca purāṇi sanniviṣṭāni parvata antargatāni ca su sambaddhāni ca anyonyam eka dvārāṇi ca anyathā dīrgha śmaśru dharā ātmānaḥ nīlāḥ megha sama prabhāḥ jāta mātrāḥ prajāḥ tatra aśīti parama āyuṣaḥ śākhāmṛga sadharmāṇaḥ phala mūla āśinaḥ tathā go dharmāṇaḥ hi anirdiṣṭāḥ śauca ācāra vivarjitāḥ tat dvīpam tādṛśaiḥ pūrṇam manujaiḥ kṣudra mānuṣaiḥ evam ete antara dvīpāḥ vyākhyātāḥ ānupūrvaśaḥ viṃśatrriṃśat ca pañcāśat ṣaṣṭi aśītiḥ śatam tathā sahasram api ca api uktam yojanānām samantataḥ vistīrṇāḥ ca āyatāḥ ca eva nānā sattva samākulāḥ barhiṇadvīpa parvāṇi kṣudra dvīpāḥ sahasraśas jambūdvīpa pradeśāt tu ṣaṭ anye vividha āśrayāḥ atra dvīpāḥ samākhyātāḥ nānā ratna ākarāḥ kṣitau aṅga dvīpam yama dvīpam malaya
